### [1] [A parameterized block-splitting preconditioner for indefinite least squares problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16938)
*Davod Khojasteh Salkuyeh*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于块分裂的定常迭代方法来解决不定最小二乘问题，并将其作为预条件子来加速GMRES方法的收敛


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对不定最小二乘问题求解效率低的问题，需要开发更有效的迭代方法和预条件技术来提高求解速度

Method: 提出基于块分裂的定常迭代方法，分析收敛性并确定最优参数值，将该方法构造成预条件子用于加速GMRES方法，同时分析预条件矩阵的特征值分布

Result: 数值实验验证了所提出预条件子的有效性，与其他知名方法的数值比较显示了该方法的优越性

Conclusion: 基于块分裂的预条件子能够有效加速不定最小二乘问题的GMRES求解，具有良好的收敛性能和实用价值

Abstract: We present a stationary iteration based upon a block splitting for a class of
indefinite least squares problem. Convergence of the proposed method is
investigated and optimal value of the involving parameter is used. The induced
preconditioner is applied to accelerate the convergence of the GMRES method for
solving the problem. We also analysed the eigenpair distribution of the
preconditioned matrix. Some numerical are presented to show the effectiveness
of the preconditioner. Numerical comparison with other well-known methods are
also presented.

</details>


### [2] [DDFEM: A Python Package for Diffuse Domain Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16964)
*Luke Benfield,Andreas Dedner*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文介绍了ddfem，一个用于将偏微分方程转换为扩散域形式的Python包，通过相场函数在简单域上求解复杂几何域的PDE问题，并提供了处理多种边界条件的新方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在复杂域上求解偏微分方程面临巨大的计算挑战，需要一种更简单易用的方法来处理复杂几何，使扩散域方法更容易应用和实现。

Method: 开发ddfem Python包，使用扩散域方法(DDM)将PDE重新表述到更大的简单域上，通过相场函数嵌入原始几何；提供符号距离函数组合定义复杂域；引入归一化加权方法处理不同边界段的多种边界条件类型；使用统一形式语言UFL确保与现有有限元求解器的兼容性。

Result: 成功开发了ddfem包，提供了直观的复杂域定义功能和多种DDM变换器；实现了基于多个相场归一化加权的新边界条件处理方法；在Dune-Fem框架下进行了实验验证，证明了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: ddfem包为扩散域方法的应用提供了一个可扩展、易用的框架，通过相场函数和归一化加权技术，成功解决了复杂域PDE求解和多类型边界条件处理的难题，具有良好的兼容性和实用性。

Abstract: Solving partial differential equations (PDEs) on complex domains can present
significant computational challenges. The Diffuse Domain Method (DDM) is an
alternative that reformulates the partial differential equations on a larger,
simpler domain. The original geometry is embedded into the problem by
representing it with a phase-field function. This paper introduces ddfem, an
extensible Python package to provide a framework for transforming PDEs into a
Diffuse Domain formulation. We aim to make the application of a variety of
different Diffuse Domain approaches more accessible and straightforward to use.
The ddfem package includes features to intuitively define complex domains by
combining signed distance functions and provides a number of DDM transformers
for general second evolution equations. In addition, we present a new approach
for combining multiple boundary conditions of different types on distinct
boundary segments. This is achieved by applying a normalised weighting, derived
from multiple phase fields, to combine the additional boundary terms in the
Diffuse Domain formulations. The domain definition and Diffuse Domain
transformation provided by our package are designed to be compatible with a
wide range of existing finite element solvers without requiring code
alterations. Both the original (non-linear) PDEs provided by the user and the
resulting transformed PDEs on the extended domain are defined using the Unified
Form Language UFL which is a domain specific language used by a number of
software packages. Our experiments were carried out using the Dune-Fem
framework.

</details>


### [3] [Exact closure for discrete large-eddy simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17051)
*Syver Døving Agdestein,Roel Verstappen,Benjamin Sanderse*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 提出了离散大涡模拟(LES)中新的离散化一致的亚滤波应力(SFS)张量表达式，通过新的双网格滤波器精确计算SFS张量，并发现非对称部分在离散LES方程中起重要作用


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的离散LES中亚滤波应力张量表达式与离散化不一致，导致计算误差随时间增长，需要开发与离散化一致的新表达式来提高LES精度

Method: 引入具有"滤波交换"性质的新双网格滤波器，基于体积或表面平均提出三种新滤波器，推导离散化一致的对易子表达式，并使用非对称张量基闭合模型来近似新的精确SFS表达式

Result: 对于一维Burgers方程，新的离散化一致SFS表达式与常用表达式显著不同；体积平均可获得结构形式的对易子表达式但产生非对称SFS张量；包含非对称部分时，新SFS表达式在LES中给出零后验误差，而现有表达式误差随时间增长

Conclusion: 非对称SFS张量部分在离散LES方程中起重要作用，新提出的离散化一致表达式能显著提高LES计算精度，建议使用非对称张量基闭合模型来近似这些新的精确SFS表达式

Abstract: In this article we propose new discretization-consistent expressions for the
sub-filter stress (SFS) tensor in discrete LES, where the filter is induced by
the discretization. We introduce a new two-grid filter that allows us to
exactly compute the SFS tensor when DNS data is available. This new filter
satisfies a "filter-swap" property, such that filtering and finite differencing
can be interchanged and the resulting commutator expressions are of structural
form (they can be written as the discrete divergence of an SFS tensor). For 1D
conservation laws such as Burgers' equation, the resulting
discretization-consistent SFS expression is markedly different from the
commonly used (discretization-inconsistent) expression $\overline{u u} -
\bar{u} \bar{u}$. For the 3D incompressible Navier-Stokes equations, we propose
three new two-grid filters, based on either volume- or surface-averaging, each
inducing new discretization-consistent commutator expressions. We show that
volume-averaging is required to obtain a commutator expression of structural
form. However, the resulting SFS tensor is shown to be non-symmetric. Based on
DNS results, we show that the non-symmetric part of the SFS tensor plays an
important role in the discrete LES equation. When the non-symmetric part is
included, our SFS expressions give zero a-posteriori error in LES, while
existing SFS expressions give errors that increase over time. We propose to use
a class of non-symmetric tensor-basis closure models to approximate the new
exact SFS expressions.

</details>


### [4] [Matrix-Free Evaluation of High-Order Shifted Boundary Finite Element Operators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17053)
*Michał Wichrowski*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种无矩阵方法来实现有限元分析中的移位边界方法(SBM)，通过预计算数据和张量积结构高效评估移位边界算子，在d维空间中p阶多项式元素上实现了每个面O(p^{2d-1})的计算复杂度


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 移位边界方法在复杂几何形状上求解偏微分方程时需要高效的实现方式，传统的全局矩阵组装方法计算复杂度较高，需要开发避免显式矩阵组装的无矩阵方法来提高计算效率和可扩展性

Method: 采用无矩阵方法实现移位边界方法，利用预计算数据和张量积结构来高效评估移位边界算子，避免显式组装全局矩阵，适用于连续和不连续Galerkin公式的高阶有限元方法

Result: 数值实验验证了该方法的准确性和效率，实现了每个面O(p^{2d-1})的计算复杂度，其中p为多项式阶数，d为维数。与无矩阵CutFEM实现相比，展现了良好的可扩展性和适用性

Conclusion: 提出的无矩阵移位边界方法成功地在保持精度的同时显著提高了计算效率，为复杂几何形状上的高阶有限元分析提供了一种高效且可扩展的解决方案

Abstract: This paper presents a matrix-free approach for implementing the shifted
boundary method (SBM) in finite element analysis. The SBM is a versatile
technique for solving partial differential equations on complex geometries by
shifting boundary conditions to nearby surrogate boundaries. We focus on the
efficient evaluation of shifted boundary operators using precomputed data and
tensor-product structures. The proposed method avoids the explicit assembly of
global matrices, achieving a computational complexity of $O(p^{2d-1})$ per face
for the evaluation of shifted boundary contributions on elements of polynomial
degree $p$ in $d$ dimensions. Numerical experiments validate the accuracy and
efficiency of the approach, demonstrating its scalability and applicability to
high-order finite element methods for both continuous and discontinuous
Galerkin formulations. We compare the performance of the proposed method with a
matrix-free CutFEM implementation.

</details>


### [5] [Explicit Monotone Stable Super-Time-Stepping Methods for Finite Time Singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17062)
*Zheng Tan,Tariq D. Aslam,Andrea L. Bertozzi*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文探索了一种新的数值方法来解决非线性抛物型偏微分方程中有限时间奇点的标度行为问题，提出了RKL和RKG超时间步进方法，相比传统隐式方法在保持精度的同时显著减少了运行时间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多有趣的非线性偏微分方程具有有限时间奇点，扩散的存在往往限制了稳定性约束下只能使用隐式或半隐式时间步方法。有限时间奇点由于需要解析大范围的尺度而特别具有挑战性，通常需要自适应空间网格和自适应时间步。

Method: 采用Runge-Kutta-Legendre (RKL)和Runge-Kutta-Gegenbauer (RKG)超时间步进方法。这些是多阶段单步二阶前向时间方法，无需隐式求解。其优势是稳定性时间步长随阶段数s按O(s²)缩放。

Result: 通过两个非线性偏微分方程的例子展示了自相似奇点结构的时间和空间尺度可以使用RKL和RKG方法解析，无需强制使用更小的时间步。相比常用的隐式数值方法，在保持相当精度的同时显著减少了运行时间。

Conclusion: 证明了RKL和RKG方法在常系数热方程的线性稳定性条件下（无限域和周期边界条件情况）具有数值单调性，为RKL和RKG方法相对于传统超时间步进方法（如RKC和ROCK方法）的优越性提供了理论保证。

Abstract: We explore a novel way to numerically resolve the scaling behavior of
finite-time singularities in solutions of nonlinear parabolic PDEs. The
Runge--Kutta--Legendre (RKL) and Runge--Kutta--Gegenbauer (RKG)
super-time-stepping methods were originally developed for nonlinear complex
physics problems with diffusion. These are multi-stage single step
second-order, forward-in-time methods with no implicit solves. The advantage is
that the timestep size for stability scales with stage number $s$ as
$\mathcal{O}(s^2)$. Many interesting nonlinear PDEs have finite-time
singularities, and the presence of diffusion often limits one to using implicit
or semi-implicit timestep methods for stability constraints. Finite-time
singularities are particularly challenging due to the large range of scales
that one desires to resolve, often with adaptive spatial grids and adaptive
timesteps. Here we show two examples of nonlinear PDEs for which the
self-similar singularity structure has time and space scales that are
resolvable using the RKL and RKG methods, without forcing even smaller
timesteps. Compared to commonly-used implicit numerical methods, we achieve
significantly smaller run time while maintaining comparable accuracy. We also
prove numerical monotonicity for both the RKL and RKG methods under their
linear stability conditions for the constant coefficient heat equation, in the
case of infinite domain and periodic boundary condition, leading to a
theoretical guarantee of the superiority of the RKL and RKG methods over
traditional super-time-stepping methods, such as the Runge-Kutta-Chebyshev
(RKC) and the orthogonal Runge-Kutta-Chebyshev (ROCK) methods.

</details>


### [6] [Design and analysis of twisted and BGG Stokes-de Rham polytopal complexes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17333)
*Daniele A. Di Pietro,Jérôme Droniou,Kaibo Hu,Arax Leroy*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 基于DDR框架在多边形网格上设计离散BGG图，构建了适用于通用多边形网格的新型弹性复形，并建立了完整的同调和解析性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在通用多边形网格上构建具有良好数学性质的弹性复形，解决现有方法在处理复杂几何时的局限性。

Method: 基于DDR（离散德拉姆）框架设计离散Bernstein-Gelfand-Gelfand (BGG)图，该图由离散Stokes多边形复形和张量化离散德拉姆复形组成。

Result: 成功构建了适用于通用多边形网格的弹性复形，建立了离散Stokes复形的完整同调和解析性质，包括原始和伴随一致性估计以及Poincaré不等式，同时确立了从BGG图构建的复形的同调性质。

Conclusion: 通过DDR框架成功实现了在多边形网格上的离散BGG构造，为弹性问题提供了具有严格数学基础的数值方法，扩展了复形方法在计算力学中的应用范围。

Abstract: We design a discrete Bernstein--Gelfand--Gelfand (BGG) diagram on polygonal
meshes based on the DDR framework; the diagram is made of a discrete Stokes
polygonal complex and a tensorised Discrete De Rham complex, and the BGG
construction leads to a novel elasticity complex applicable on generic
polygonal meshes. Complete homological and analytical properties of the
discrete Stokes complex are established, including primal and adjoint
consistency estimates as well as Poincar\'e inequalities. Homological
properties of the complexes built from the BGG diagram are also established.

</details>


### [7] [An FDM-sFEM scheme on time-space manifolds and its superconvergence analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17378)
*Chengrun Jiang,Guozhi Dong,Hailong Guo,Zuoqiang Shi*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 研究了时空乘积流形上拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的超收敛离散化方法，提出了时间有限差分与空间表面有限元相结合的耦合格式，通过后处理技术实现梯度的超收敛恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对一般曲面上动态最优传输问题中出现的时空乘积流形上带诺伊曼时间边界条件的拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子离散化问题，需要开发高精度的数值方法。

Method: 提出了一种耦合格式，结合时间方向的有限差分方法和空间方向的表面有限元方法；建立了新的分部求和公式；基于黎曼度量近似的新框架进行几何误差分析；采用后处理技术恢复梯度。

Result: 证明了半离散解的超逼近性质；通过后处理技术导出了恢复梯度的超收敛结果；提供了多个数值算例验证理论结果。

Conclusion: 成功开发了时空乘积流形上拉普拉斯-贝尔特拉米算子的超收敛离散化方法，理论分析和数值实验都验证了方法的有效性，为动态最优传输等应用提供了高精度的数值工具。

Abstract: We study superconvergent discretization of the Laplace-Beltrami operator on
time-space product manifolds with Neumann temporal boundary values, which arise
in the context of dynamic optimal transport on general surfaces. We propose a
coupled scheme that combines finite difference methods in time with surface
finite element methods in space. By establishing a new summation by parts
formula and proving the supercloseness of the semi-discrete solution, we derive
superconvergence results for the recovered gradient via post-processing
techniques. In addition, our geometric error analysis is implemented within a
novel framework based on the approximation of the Riemannian metric. Several
numerical examples are provided to validate and illustrate the theoretical
results.

</details>


### [8] [Univariate amenable functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17404)
*Carlos Beltrán*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对单变量实解析函数发展了适宜函数和兼容函数的理论，提供了简单的测试方法并为基本函数制作了适宜性表格


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了建立精确的数学定理来保证后向稳定算法也是前向稳定的，以及两个稳定算法的组合仍然是稳定的，需要发展适宜函数和兼容函数的理论

Method: 针对单变量实解析函数，为适宜函数和兼容函数概念提供简单的测试方法，并对一系列基本函数进行分析

Result: 为多个基本函数制作了适宜性表格，明确了哪些函数是适宜的，哪些不是适宜的

Conclusion: 通过为单变量实解析函数发展适宜函数和兼容函数理论，提供了实用的测试工具和基本函数的适宜性分类表格

Abstract: The concepts of amenable and compatible functions have been introduced in a
recent work, in order to state precise mathematical theorems that guarantee
that a backward stable algorithm is also forward stable, and that the
composition of two stable algorithms results in an stable algorithm. In this
work, we elaborate in this theory for univariate real analytic functions,
providing simple tests for both concepts and producing tables for a number of
elementary functions which are or fail to be amenable.

</details>


### [9] [A new data-driven energy-stable Evolve-Filter-Relax model for turbulent flow simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17423)
*Anna Ivagnes,Toby van Gastelen,Syver Døving Agdestein,Benjamin Sanderse,Giovanni Stabile,Gianluigi Rozza*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种数据驱动的方法来改进EFR（演化-滤波-松弛）框架中的滤波和松弛步骤，通过在频域基于DNS数据学习最优滤波器，显著提高了湍流模拟的精度和计算效率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EFR框架虽然实现简单且计算高效，但由于只包含两个参数（一个用于滤波步骤，一个用于松弛步骤），其灵活性受到限制，需要一种更优的方法来确定滤波器和松弛参数以提高湍流模拟的准确性。

Method: 提出了一种数据驱动的方法，在频域基于DNS数据寻找最优滤波器。优化过程计算高效，仅涉及每个波数的一维最小二乘问题。松弛参数通过要求能量和/或涡度守恒来确定，以确保方法的稳定性并减少数值振荡。

Result: 在衰减湍流和Kolmogorov流两种情况下，学习得到的滤波器明显优于标准微分滤波器和Smagorinsky模型，在能量谱以及能量和涡度的时间演化方面都显著提高了精度。应用学习滤波器比传统微分滤波器计算效率更高，因为它避免了求解线性系统。

Conclusion: 数据驱动的EFR方法通过在频域学习最优滤波器和基于守恒定律确定松弛参数，成功提高了湍流模拟的精度和计算效率，为湍流数值模拟提供了一种更加灵活和有效的方法。

Abstract: We present a novel approach to define the filter and relax steps in the
evolve-filter-relax (EFR) framework for simulating turbulent flows. The EFR
main advantages are its ease of implementation and computational efficiency.
However, as it only contains two parameters (one for the filter step and one
for the relax step) its flexibility is rather limited. In this work, we propose
a data-driven approach in which the optimal filter is found based on DNS data
in the frequency domain. The optimization step is computationally efficient and
only involves one-dimensional least-squares problems for each wavenumber.
Across both decaying turbulence and Kolmogorov flow, our learned filter
decisively outperforms the standard differential filter and the Smagorinsky
model, yielding significantly improved accuracy in energy spectra and in the
temporal evolution of both energy and enstrophy. In addition, the relax
parameter is determined by requiring energy and/or enstrophy conservation,
which enforces stability of the method and reduces the appearance of numerical
wiggles, especially when the filter is built in scarce data regimes. Applying
the learned filter is also more computationally efficient compared to
traditional differential filters, as it circumvents solving a linear system.

</details>


### [10] [Error estimates and adaptivity for a least-squares method applied to the Monge-Ampère equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17569)
*Alexandre Caboussat,Anna Peruso,Marco Picasso*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文针对凸多边形域上Monge-Ampère方程的光滑解，提出了一种非线性最小二乘求解器的新颖后验误差指示器，并设计了鲁棒的自适应网格细化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Monge-Ampère方程的数值求解开发有效的后验误差估计和自适应网格细化方法，以提高求解精度和计算效率。该方程在最优传输、微分几何等领域有重要应用，但其非线性特性使得误差控制具有挑战性。

Method: 采用迭代求解方案，将问题解耦为：(1)逐点非线性最小化问题；(2)线性双调和变分问题。对于双调和问题，建立了与Navier边界条件双调和问题的等价性，并使用混合分片线性有限元求解。将其重新表述为耦合二阶系统，推导了P1有限元的先验和后验误差估计器。

Result: 数值测试确认了不同范数下误差的适当缩放性质。后验误差指示器在指导网格细化方面表现出有效性，验证了所提出的自适应网格细化策略的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 成功开发了针对Monge-Ampère方程的后验误差指示器和自适应网格细化策略。该方法通过问题解耦和等价性建立，实现了有效的误差控制，为该类非线性椭圆方程的数值求解提供了可靠的计算框架。

Abstract: We introduce novel a posteriori error indicators for a nonlinear
least-squares solver for smooth solutions of the Monge--Amp\`ere equation on
convex polygonal domains in $\mathbb{R}^2$. At each iteration, our iterative
scheme decouples the problem into (i) a pointwise nonlinear minimization
problem and (ii) a linear biharmonic variational problem. For the latter, we
derive an equivalence to a biharmonic problem with Navier boundary conditions
and solve it via mixed piecewise-linear finite elements. Reformulating this as
a coupled second-order system, we derive a priori and a posteriori
$\mathbb{P}^1$ finite element error estimators and we design a robust adaptive
mesh refinement strategy. Numerical tests confirm that errors in different
norms scale appropriately. Finally, we demonstrate the effectiveness of our a
posteriori indicators in guiding mesh refinement.

Abstract: Iterative solvers for large-scale linear systems such as Krylov subspace

for high-performance computing solutions of such large-scale linear systems. To

method are also presented as comparison. Varying numbers of grid points are
employed in each case to assess the behavior and accuracy of both the neural
network and the finite difference method. The experimental results demonstrate
that the proposed neural network produces better solutions, generates more
accurate bifurcation diagrams, has reasonable computational times, and proves
effective for linear stability analysis.

### [13] [Data assimilation using a global Girsanov nudged particle filter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17685)
*Maneesh Kumar Singh,Joshua Hope-Collins,Colin J. Cotter,Dan Crisan*

Main category: math.NA

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有粒子滤波方法在处理无限维状态空间的随机模型时存在困难，需要开发新的算法来维持良好的有效样本量(ESS)并提高滤波性能

Method: 使用Girsanov扰动的粒子滤波算法，将最优控制问题分解为三个阶段：分离ESS项中的非线性与前向问题的非线性，允许在控制变量空间中对每个粒子进行独立并行计算

Result: 在随机Kuramoto-Sivashinsky方程上的实验表明，相比于temper-jitter粒子滤波方法，推进滤波器虽然过度分散，但能更快速、更稳健地响应同化数据中的极端事件

Conclusion: 提出的推进粒子滤波算法在处理无限维随机系统时具有优势，特别是在响应极端事件方面表现更佳，为无限维状态空间的数据同化提供了新的有效方法

Abstract: We present a particle filtering algorithm for stochastic models on infinite
dimensional state space, making use of Girsanov perturbations to nudge the
ensemble of particles into regions of higher likelihood. We argue that the
optimal control problem needs to couple control variables for all of the
particles to maintain an ensemble with good effective sample size (ESS). We
provide an optimisation formulation that separates the problem into three
stages, separating the nonlinearity in the ESS term in the functional with the
nonlinearity due to the forward problem, and allowing independent parallel
computation for each particle when calculations are performed over control
variable space. The particle filter is applied to the stochastic
Kuramoto-Sivashinsky equation, and compared with the temper-jitter particle
filter approach. We observe that whilst the nudging filter is over spread
compared to the temper-jitter filter, it responds to extreme events in the
assimilated data more quickly and robustly.

### [14] [The Generalized Matrix Separation Problem: Algorithms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17069)
*Xuemei Chen,Owen Deen*

Main category: math.OC

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的广义矩阵分离问题需要从观测矩阵M₀=L₀+HS₀中恢复低秩矩阵L₀和稀疏矩阵S₀，虽然已有凸优化理论框架（ℓ₁范数和核范数之和），但缺乏高效的算法实现策略，特别是针对不同矩阵结构（循环、可分离、块结构）的优化方法。

Method: 详细设计了求解凸优化问题的迭代算法及其计算过程，针对H矩阵的不同结构特性（循环矩阵、可分离矩阵、块结构矩阵）提出了多种高效实现策略，并开发了一种预处理技术来改善算法性能。

Result: 提出的预处理技术在效率、精度和鲁棒性方面显著改善了算法性能，数值实验验证了所提方法的有效性，并为预处理策略提供了理论保证。

Conclusion: 本文成功开发了广义矩阵分离问题的高效算法实现框架，特别是预处理技术的引入大幅提升了算法性能，为实际应用提供了可靠的计算工具和理论支撑。

Abstract: When given a generalized matrix separation problem, which aims to recover a
low rank matrix $L_0$ and a sparse matrix $S_0$ from $M_0=L_0+HS_0$, the work
\cite{CW25} proposes a novel convex optimization problem whose objective
function is the sum of the $\ell_1$-norm and nuclear norm. In this paper we
detail the iterative algorithms and its associated computations for solving
this convex optimization problem. We present various efficient implementation
strategies, with attention to practical cases where $H$ is circulant,
separable, or block structured. Notably, we propose a preconditioning technique
that drastically improved the performance of our algorithms in terms of
efficiency, accuracy, and robustness. While this paper serves as an
illustrative algorithm implementation manual, we also provide theoretical
guarantee for our preconditioning strategy. Numerical results illustrate the
effectiveness of the proposed approach.

</details>

### [16] [Frank-Wolfe algorithm for star-convex functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17272)
*R. Diaz Millan,Orizon Pereira Ferreira,Julien Ugon*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了Frank-Wolfe算法在星凸函数上的应用，证明了即使在非凸设置下，该算法仍能保持O(1/k)的最优复杂度界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典的Frank-Wolfe算法复杂度分析主要集中在凸函数上，但现实中许多优化问题涉及非凸函数。为了扩展算法的适用范围，需要研究在保持某些几何性质的非凸函数类（如星凸函数）上的性能表现。

Method: 针对星凸函数类，分析Frank-Wolfe算法在紧凸集上最小化具有Lipschitz连续梯度的可微函数。采用三种步长策略：递减步长、Armijo型步长和基于Lipschitz常数的步长规则，建立相应的迭代复杂度界限。

Result: 在星凸性假设下，对于目标函数值和对偶间隙都建立了O(1/k)的迭代复杂度界限。特别地，递减步长和Armijo策略不需要事先知道Lipschitz常数或曲率常数，增强了算法的实用性。

Conclusion: Frank-Wolfe方法在超越凸设置的情况下仍能保持最优的复杂度保证，为非凸优化提供了理论支撑，扩展了该算法的应用范围。

Abstract: We study the Frank-Wolfe algorithm for minimizing a differentiable function
with Lipschitz continuous gradient over a compact convex set. To extend
classical complexity bounds to certain non-convex functions, we focus on the
class of \emph{star-convex functions}, which retain essential geometric
properties despite the lack of convexity. We establish iteration-complexity
bounds of $\mathcal{O}(1/k)$ for both the objective values and the duality gap
under star-convexity, using diminishing, Armijo-type, and Lipschitz-based
stepsize rules. Notably, the diminishing and Armijo strategies do not require
prior knowledge of Lipschitz or curvature constants. These results demonstrate
that the Frank-Wolfe method preserves optimal complexity guarantees beyond the
convex setting.

</details>

the accelerating shift towards EVs. This comprehensive review aims to
thoroughly examine current global practices in EVCI planning and explore
state-of-the-art methodologies for designing EVCI planning strategies. Despite
remarkable efforts by influential players in the global EV market, such as
China, the United States, and the European Union, the progress in EVCI rollout
has been notably slower than anticipated in the rest of the world. This delay
can be attributable to three major impediments: inadequate EVCI charging

Motivation: 现有的有限和优化问题求解方法计算成本过高，需要开发能够显著降低计算复杂度的高效算法。传统信赖域方法在处理大规模问题时需要计算完整的梯度和海塞矩阵，计算代价昂贵。

Method: 开发了基于子采样策略的信赖域方法，用子采样来近似目标函数的梯度和海塞矩阵。提出了一种新颖的自适应程序，能够确定性地调整用于梯度（或梯度和海塞矩阵）近似的样本大小。

Result: 建立了获得近似平稳点的最坏情况迭代复杂度界限：对于ε_g-近似一阶平稳点，最多需要O(ε_g^{-2})次迭代；对于(ε_g,ε_H)-近似二阶平稳点，最多需要O(max{ε_g^{-2}ε_H^{-1}, ε_H^{-3}})次迭代。数值实验验证了新子采样技术的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的子采样信赖域方法能够有效解决有限和优化问题，在保证理论收敛保证的同时显著降低了计算成本。自适应采样策略和建立的复杂度界限为该方法的实际应用提供了理论支撑。

Abstract: In this paper, we develop and analyze sub-sampled trust-region methods for
solving finite-sum optimization problems. These methods employ subsampling
strategies to approximate the gradient and Hessian of the objective function,
significantly reducing the overall computational cost. We propose a novel
adaptive procedure for deterministically adjusting the sample size used for
gradient (or gradient and Hessian) approximations. Furthermore, we establish
worst-case iteration complexity bounds for obtaining approximate stationary
points. More specifically, for a given $\varepsilon_g, \varepsilon_H\in (0,1)$,
it is shown that an $\varepsilon_g$-approximate first-order stationary point is
reached in at most $\mathcal{O}({\varepsilon_g}^{-2} )$ iterations, whereas an
$(\varepsilon_g,\varepsilon_H)$-approximate second-order stationary point is
reached in at most
$\mathcal{O}(\max\{\varepsilon_{g}^{-2}\varepsilon_{H}^{-1},\varepsilon_{H}^{-3}\})$
iterations. Finally, numerical experiments illustrate the effectiveness of our
new subsampling technique.

</details>


### [20] [A Compact Cycle Formulation for the Multiperiodic Event Scheduling Problem](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17566)
*Rolf Nelson van Lieshout,Niels Lindner*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文研究了多周期事件调度问题（MPESP），这是周期性公共交通时刻表编制中PESP的推广版本，允许每个事件有自己的独立周期。作者提出了基于循环的新公式化方法，能够处理异构服务频率，在大规模实际公共交通网络上表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的公共交通网络往往具有异构的服务频率，而传统的周期性事件调度问题（PESP）假设所有事件共享一个公共周期，无法很好地建模这种异构性。因此需要开发能够处理每个事件具有独立周期的多周期事件调度问题（MPESP）。

Method: 提出了MPESP的基于循环的公式化方法，扩展了PESP的最强已知公式。该方法需要从满足特定结构属性的生成树派生循环基础，将尖锐生成树的概念扩展到有根实例。证明了循环周期性性质的多周期类比，并算法性地构造所需的结构。

Result: 新公式化方法几乎解决了所有测试实例，包括几个大规模现实世界公共交通网络，达到最优解或具有较小的最优性间隙，显著优于现有的基于弧的模型。

Conclusion: MPESP在捕获异构频率方面显示出实际潜力，无需诉诸人工事件复制。基于循环的新公式化方法为处理多周期性问题提供了有效的解决方案，在实际公共交通网络优化中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: The Periodic Event Scheduling Problem (PESP) is a fundamental model in
periodic timetabling for public transport systems, assuming a common period
across all events. However, real-world networks often feature heterogeneous
service frequencies. This paper studies the Multiperiodic Event Scheduling
Problem (MPESP), a generalization of PESP that allows each event to recur at
its own individual period. While more expressive, MPESP presents new modeling
challenges due to the loss of a global period. We present a cycle-based
formulation for MPESP that extends the strongest known formulation for PESP
and, in contrast to existing approaches, is valid for any MPESP instance.
Crucially, the formulation requires a cycle basis derived from a spanning tree
satisfying specific structural properties, which we formalize and
algorithmically construct, extending the concept of sharp spanning trees to
rooted instances. We further prove a multiperiodic analogue of the cycle
periodicity property. Our new formulation solves nearly all tested instances,
including several large-scale real-world public transport networks, to
optimality or with small optimality gaps, dramatically outperforming existing
arc-based models. The results demonstrate the practical potential of MPESP in
capturing heterogeneous frequencies without resorting to artificial event
duplication.

### [21] [How orthogonality influences geometric constants?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17122)
*Yuxin Wang,Qi Liu,Mengmeng Bao*

Main category: math.FA

TL;DR: 本文基于等腰正交性，发现了三个几何常数A2(X)、CNJ(X)和LYJ(X)的等价定义，这些常数都限制在单位球面上，揭示了在正交条件下整个空间上定义的常数可能等价于限制在单位球面上的常数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于等腰正交性理论，对三个几何常数A2(X)（2000年Baronti提出）、CNJ(X)（2008年Alonso等人引入）和LYJ(X)（2022年Liu等人提出）进行分析，寻找它们的等价定义。

Result: 成功找到了三个几何常数A2(X)、CNJ(X)和LYJ(X)基于等腰正交性的等价定义，证明了这些常数在单位球面上的限制性质。

Conclusion: 三个几何常数A2(X)、CNJ(X)和LYJ(X)都具有限制在单位球面上的核心共性，这为理解几何常数的本质提供了新的洞察，即在正交条件下，整个空间上定义的常数可能等价于限制在单位球面上的常数。

Abstract: In this paper, based on isosceles orthogonality, we have found equivalent
definitions for three constants: A2(X) proposed by Baronti in 2000 [J. Math.
Anal. Appl. 252(2000), 124- 146], CNJ(X) introduced by Alonso et al. in 2008
[Stud. Math. 188(2008), 135-150], and LYJ(X) put forward by Liu et al. in 2022
[Bull. Malays. Math. Sci. Soc., 45(2022), 307-321]. A core commonality among
these three constants is that they are all restricted to the unit sphere. This
finding provides us with an insight: could it be that several constants defined
over the entire space, when combined with orthogonality conditions, are
equivalent to being restricted to the unit sphere?

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过建立范数乘积公式与权重正则性条件之间的等价关系，证明对于n≥2的情况下，张量积的范数等于各个算子范数的乘积当且仅当权重满足正则性条件。

Result: 证明了范数乘积公式成立的充要条件是权重满足正则性条件，并且发现包括加权Bergman移位、Hardy移位、Dirichlet移位等在内的大多数函数空间上的加权移位算子都满足正则性条件。

Abstract: In the present paper, we study the norms for symmetric and antisymmetric
tensor products of weighted shift operators. By proving that for $n\geq 2$,
  $$\|S_{\alpha}^{l_1}\odot\cdots \odot S_{\alpha}^{l_k}\odot
S_{\alpha}^{*l_{k+1}}\odot\cdots \odot S_{\alpha}^{*l_{n}}\|
=\mathop{\prod}_{i=1}^n\left \| S_{\alpha}^{{l_{i}}}\right\|, \text{ for any} \
(l_1,l_2\cdots l_n)\in\mathbb N^n$$ if and only if the weight satisfies the
regularity condition, we partially solve \cite[Problem 6 and Problem 7]{GA}. It
will be seen that most weighted shift operators on function spaces, including
weighted Bergman shift, Hardy shift, Dirichlet shift, etc, satisfy the
regularity condition. Moreover, at the end of the paper, we solve \cite[Problem
1 and Problem 2]{GA}.

### [24] [Cyclic Operators, Linear Functionals and RKHS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17358)
*Yi Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，算子的"近次正规性质"通过线性泛函的正性来研究。本文希望从一个新的角度——即线性泛函何时由紧支撑分布给出——来探讨这些性质，并寻找算子模型的不同方法。

Method: 通过分析二变量核函数的非对角增长条件来判断线性泛函是否由紧支撑分布给出；利用核函数定义的再生核希尔伯特空间构建循环交换算子元组的函数模型；在构造中使用Fock空间的再生核，但也可以用其他再生核希尔伯特空间替代。

Result: 得到了线性泛函由紧支撑分布给出的充要条件，即二变量核函数的非对角增长条件；成功构建了所有循环交换算子元组的函数模型；提供了多个具体例子验证理论结果。

Conclusion: 本文为研究算子的"近次正规性质"提供了新的视角和方法，通过再生核希尔伯特空间理论建立了算子模型的新途径，这种方法具有一般性且可以推广到其他再生核希尔伯特空间。

Abstract: Given a commuting $n$-tuple of bounded linear operators on a Hilbert space,
together with a distinguished cyclic vector, Jim Agler defined a linear
functional $\Lambda_{\mathbf{T},h}$ on the polynomial ring
$\mathbb{C}[\mathbf{z},\bar{\mathbf{z}}]$. ``Near subnormality properties'' of
an operator $T$ are translated into positivity properties of $\Lambda_{T,h}$.
In this paper, we approach ``near subnormality properties'' in a different way
by answering the following question: when is $\Lambda_{\mathbf{T},h}$ given by
a compactly supported distribution? The answer is in terms of the off-diagonal
growth condition of a two-variable kernel function $F_{\mathbf{T},h}$ on
$\mathbb{C}^n$. Using the reproducing kernel Hilbert spaces (RKHS) defined by
the kernel function $F_{\mathbf{T},h}$, we give a function model for all cyclic
commuting $n$-tuples. This potentially gives a different approach to operator
models. The reproducing kernels of the Fock space are used in the construction
of $F_{\mathbf{T},h}$, but one may also replace the Fock space by other RKHS.
We give many examples in the last section.

Result: 通过广义特征分析得出了九种拓扑不同的解模式，其中一些配置表现出类似马赫反射的特征，在某些情况下还可能出现真空区域。数值模拟结果与理论分析结果吻合良好。

Conclusion: 成功构建了二维无压欧拉方程中涉及接触间断和δ激波相互作用的完整解结构分类，理论分析与数值验证的一致性证明了所提出方法的有效性，为理解复杂波相互作用现象提供了重要的理论基础。

Abstract: In this article, we investigate the two-dimensional pressureless Euler

distinguishing feature of the solution is the emergence of a delta shock wave
which is characterized by a Dirac delta function appearing in both the density
and internal energy variables. By exploiting generalized characteristic
analysis, nine topologically distinct solution patterns are derived. Some of
these configurations exhibit features similar to Mach-reflection and in certain
cases, vacuum regions may also develop. To validate the theoretical results,
numerical simulations are carried out using a semidiscrete central upwind
scheme. The comparison between analytical and numerical results demonstrates
excellent agreement, providing

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究高度各向异性的二维单位向量场能量泛函在极限情况下的性质，特别是当参数ε趋于0时，能量泛函对向量场梯度控制能力的变化

Method: 采用双曲守恒律的工具来分析能量泛函，研究有界能量序列的紧性性质，并通过构造反例来证明最优性结果

Result: 证明了有界能量序列在W^{s,3}_loc(Ω)空间中对s<1/2是紧的，1/2阶可微性是最优的，边界迹在L^1(∂Ω)中具有紧性，并刻画了单变量映射和薄膜模型情况下的Γ-极限

Conclusion: 虽然各向异性能量在ε→0时失去对完整梯度的控制，但仍保持对1/2阶导数的控制，这种控制程度是最优的，为理解此类变分问题的极限行为提供了理论基础

Abstract: We study the highly anisotropic energy of two-dimensional unit vector fields
given by \begin{align*} E_\epsilon(u)= \int_{\Omega} (\mathrm{div}\,u)^2 +
\epsilon(\mathrm{curl}\,u)^2\, dx\,, \quad u\colon\Omega\subset\mathbb
R^2\to\mathbb S^1\, \end{align*}
  in the limit $\epsilon\to 0$. This energy clearly loses control on the full
gradient of $u$ as $\epsilon\to 0$, but, adapting tools from hyperbolic
conservations laws, we show that it still controls derivatives of order 1/2. In
particular, any bounded energy sequence $E_\epsilon(u_\epsilon)\leq C$ is
compact in $W^{s,3}_{\mathrm{loc}}(\Omega)$ for $s<1/2$. Moreover, this order
1/2 of differentiability is optimal, in the sense that any map $u\in
W^{1/2,4}(\Omega;\mathbb S^1)$ is a limit of a bounded energy sequence. We also
establish compactness of boundary traces in $L^1(\partial\Omega)$, and
characterize the $\Gamma$-limit in the simpler case of maps of a single
variable and in the case of a thin-film model.

### [33] [Stable self-similar singularity formation for infinite energy solutions of the incompressible porous medium equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17381)
*Charles Collot,Christophe Prange,Jin Tan*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究无粘不可压缩多孔介质方程的无限能量解的稳定性，通过变量变换将有限时间爆破解的研究转化为Proudman-Johnson方程全局解的研究，证明了显式自相似爆破解的稳定性并确定了临界正则性阈值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Castro-Córdoba-Gancedo-Orive等人引入的无粘不可压缩多孔介质方程(IPM)中一类特殊的无限能量解，特别是其显式自相似爆破解的稳定性问题，这类解在理论上具有重要意义。

Method: 采用变量变换的方法，将有限时间爆破解的研究转化为Proudman-Johnson方程的全局时间解的研究。Proudman-Johnson方程是二维Euler方程和无粘原始方程特殊解类的约化方程。通过分析这个约化方程稳态解的渐近稳定性来研究原问题。

Result: 证明了显式自相似爆破解在足够光滑扰动下的稳定性，并确定了一个尖锐的正则性阈值，低于该阈值时解是不稳定的。主要结果是Proudman-Johnson方程稳态解族的渐近稳定性及其衰减估计。

Conclusion: 通过变量变换技术成功建立了IPM方程爆破解与Proudman-Johnson方程全局解之间的联系，证明了显式爆破解的稳定性，同时该结果也适用于相关的Euler方程和无粘原始方程解类的稳定性分析。

Abstract: We consider a special class of infinite energy solutions to the inviscid
incompressible porous medium equations (IPM), introduced in
Castro-C\'ordoba-Gancedo-Orive [9]. The (IPM) equations then reduce to a
one-dimensional nonlocal nonlinear equation, for which an explicit self-similar
blow-up solution is found in [9]. We show the stability of this explicit
blow-up solution by smooth enough perturbations, and identity a sharp
regularity threshold below which it is unstable. The heart of our proof is a
change of variables that transforms the study of finite time blow-up solutions,
to the study of global-in-time solutions to the Proudman-Johnson equation,
which is a reduced equation that appears for special classes of solutions of
the two-dimensional Euler equations, and of the inviscid primitive equations
(or hydrostatic Euler equations). Our main result is in fact the asymptotic
stability with decay estimates for a family of steady states of this reduced
equation. It thus also implies the corresponding stability of steady states for
the associated classes of solutions to the Euler equations and inviscid
primitive equations.

  i\partial_t u + \partial_x^2 u = |u|^4 u,
  u(0, x) = u_0 \in L_x^2(\Bbb R).
  \] The global well-posedness and scattering for this equation was solved in
Dodson [Amer. J. Math. (2016)]. Inspired by the pioneering work of
Killip-Visan-Zhang [Amer. J. Math. (2021)], we show that solution can be
approximated by a finite-dimensional Hamiltonian system. This system is the
nonlinear Schr\"odinger equation on the rescaled torus $\Bbb R/(L_n\Bbb Z)$
with Fourier truncated nonlinear term. To prove this, we introduce the Fourier
truncated mass-critical NLS on $\mathbb{R}$. First, we establish the uniformly
global space-time bound for this truncated model on $\mathbb{R}$. Second, we

truncated nonlinearity and a single equation in $\mathbb{R}$, which can be done
by performing the nonlinear profile decomposition.
  Our second result is to study the homogenization of the mass-critical
inhomogeneous NLS, where we add a $L^\infty$ function $h(nx)$ in front of the
nonlinear term. Based on the method of Ntekoume [Comm. PDE, (2020)], we give
the sufficient condition on $h$ such that the scattering holds for this
inhomogeneous model and show that the solution to inhomogeneous converges to
the homogeneous model when $n\to\infty$. As a corollary, we can transfer the
non-squeezing property from homogeneous model to inhomogeneous.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前对于Majda-Biello系统(α=4)的研究中，局部适定性的临界指标为3/4，但全局适定性只在s≥1时得到证明。本研究旨在填补这一空白，在更低的Sobolev正则性条件下建立全局适定性。

Method: 引入一对不同的I-算子，专门针对α=4时Majda-Biello系统的共振结构设计。通过双算子框架结合多线性修正技术构造修正能量，实现对乘子的逐点控制。这些修正能量几乎守恒，为解的Sobolev范数提供有效的全局时间控制。

Result: 成功建立了Sobolev正则性s∈[3/4,1)范围内Majda-Biello系统的全局适定性，使得全局理论的阈值与局部理论完全匹配。

Abstract: We study the Cauchy problem for the following Majda-Biello system in the case
$\alpha=4$, which has the most significant resonance effect, on the real line.
\[ \left\{ \begin{array}{l}
  u_{t} + u_{xxx} = - v v_x,
  v_{t} + \alpha v_{xxx} = - (uv)_{x},
  (u,v)|_{t=0} = (u_0,v_0) \in H^{s}(\mathbb{R}) \times H^{s}(\mathbb{R}),
\end{array} \right. \quad x \in \mathbb{R}, \, t \in \mathbb{R}. \] For Sobolev
regularity $s\in[\frac34, 1)$, we establish the global well-posedness by
refining the I-method. Previously, the critical index for the local
well-posedness was known to be $\frac34$, while the global well-posedness was
only obtained for $s\geq 1$. Our global well-posedness result bridges the gap
and matches the threshold in the local theory. The main novelty of our approach
is to introduce a pair of distinct $I$-operators, tailored to the resonant
structure of the Majda-Biello system with $\alpha=4$. This dual-operator
framework allows for pointwise control of the multipliers in the modified
energies constructed via the multilinear correction technique. These modified
energies are almost conserved and provide effective control over the Sobolev
norm of the solution globally in time. This new approach has potential
applications to other coupled dispersive systems exhibiting strong resonant
interactions.

*Maciej Kucharski,Mateusz Kwaśnicki,Błażej Wróbel*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 研究高阶Riesz变换及其截断版本在不同Lp空间中的范数关系，通过分析因子化算子的性质揭示了高阶情况下的复杂行为


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解高阶Riesz变换Rk与其截断版本Rk^t之间的关系，特别是在不同Lp空间(p=1,2,∞)中的范数比较，这对于奇异积分理论具有重要意义

Method: 通过引入因子化算子Mk^t(满足Rk^t=Mk^t Rk)来分析问题，该算子是与L1径向核bk,d^t相关的卷积算子。研究核函数bk,d的性质，包括其非负性、L1范数行为以及Fourier变换的有界性

Result: 证明了bk,d≥0仅在k=1,2时成立；对于固定的k≥3，当维数d趋于无穷时‖bk,d‖L1趋于无穷，这与k=1,2时‖bk,d‖L1=1的情况形成对比；证明了对任意正整数k，bk,d的Fourier变换的绝对值有界于1

Conclusion: 建立了收缩性估计‖Rk^t f‖L2≤‖Rk f‖L2，并将类似估计推广到具有光滑核的一般奇异积分在径向输入函数上的情况。结果揭示了高阶Riesz变换(k≥3)与低阶情况(k=1,2)的本质差异

Abstract: Fix a positive integer $k$. Let $R_k$ be a higher order Riesz transform of
order $k$ on $\mathbb{R}^d$ and let $R_k^t,$ $t>0,$ be the corresponding
truncated Riesz transform. We study the relation between $\|R_k
f\|_{L^p(\mathbb{R}^d)}$ and $\|R_k^t f\|_{L^p(\mathbb{R}^d)}$ for $p=1$,
$p=\infty,$ and $p=2.$ This is performed via analysis of the factorization
operator $M_k^t$ defined by the relation $R_k^t=M_k^t R_k.$ The operator
$M_k^t$ is a convolution operator associated with an $L^1$ radial kernel
$b_{k,d}^t(x)=t^{-d}b_{k,d}(x/t),$ where $b_{k,d}(x):=b_{k,d}^1(x).$
  We prove that $b_{k,d} \ge 0$ only for $k=1,2.$ We also justify that for
fixed $k\ge 3$ it holds \[ \lim_{d\to
\infty}\|b_{k,d}\|_{L^1(\mathbb{R}^d)}=\infty. \] This is contrary to the cases
$k=1,2$ where it is known that $\|b_{k,d}\|_{L^1(\mathbb{R}^d)}=1$. Finally, we
show that for any positive integer $k$ the Fourier transform of $b_{k,d}$ is
bounded in absolute value by $1.$ This implies the contractive estimate \[
\|R_k^t f\|_{L^2(\mathbb{R}^d)}\le \|R_k f\|_{L^2(\mathbb{R}^d)} \] and an
analogous estimate for general singular integrals with smooth kernels for
radial input functions $f.$

</details>


### [41] [Bivariate multiple orthogonal polynomials of mixed type on the step-line](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17694)
*Manuel Mañas,Miguel Rojas,Jianwen Wu*

Main category: math.CA

TL;DR: 本文研究阶梯线上混合型双变量多重正交多项式，通过LU分解专门适应的矩量矩阵，确定了正交性关系、多重度数、递推关系和Christoffel-Darboux核，并建立了ABC型定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究阶梯线上混合型双变量多重正交多项式的理论性质，这是正交多项式理论的一个重要扩展，对于理解多变量正交系统具有重要意义。

Method: 基于专门适应该框架的矩量矩阵的LU分解方法，通过矩阵分析技术来研究多重正交多项式的性质。

Result: 确定了这些多项式满足的正交性和双正交性关系，获得了精确的多重度数，导出了相应的递推关系和编码它们的增长带状矩阵，得到了Christoffel-Darboux核和相关的Christoffel-Darboux型公式。

Conclusion: 建立了一个ABC型定理，该定理将截断矩量矩阵的逆与Christoffel-Darboux核联系起来，为阶梯线上混合型双变量多重正交多项式提供了完整的理论框架。

Abstract: This article studies bivariate multiple orthogonal polynomials of the mixed
type on the step-line. The analysis is based on the LU factorization of a
moment matrix specifically adapted to this framework. The orthogonality and
biorthogonality relations satisfied by these polynomials are identified, and
their precise multi-degrees are determined. The corresponding recurrence
relations and the growing band matrices that encode them are also derived.
Christoffel-Darboux kernels and the associated Christoffel-Darboux-type
formulas are obtained. An ABC-type theorem is established, relating the inverse
of the truncated moment matrix to these kernels.

numbers up to a specified bound, with potential implications for new

### [46] [Quantitative convergence for displacement monotone Mean Field Games of control](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17014)
*Joe Jackson,Alpár R. Mészáros*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究要么局限于可分离哈密顿量（使固定点映射变得平凡），要么假设固定点映射的收敛性或正则性，缺乏对MFGC中非平凡固定点问题的严格处理。需要发展新的理论框架来处理非可分离哈密顿量和措施空间上的复杂固定点问题。

Method: 对满足位移单调性条件的一般非可分离哈密顿量类别进行分析，结合温和的正则性和无穷远处增长条件。开发措施空间上固定点问题的详细结构分析，建立固定点映射的新正则性结果，并推导N玩家纳什系统的尖锐先验估计。

Result: 获得了开环均衡的定量收敛性结果，通过控制开环和闭环策略之间的差异，证明了闭环均衡的收敛性。建立了固定点映射的新正则性结果，并且框架自然地容纳了公共噪声。

Conclusion: 成功建立了MFGC设置下N玩家随机微分博弈开环和闭环纳什均衡的定量收敛理论，解决了措施空间上非平凡固定点问题，为处理非可分离哈密顿量的平均场博弈提供了严格的数学框架。

Abstract: In this paper we establish quantitative convergence results for both open and
closed-loop Nash equilibria of N-player stochastic differential games in the
setting of Mean Field Games of Controls (MFGC), a class of models where
interactions among agents occur through both states and controls. Our analysis
covers a general class of non-separable Hamiltonians satisfying a displacement
monotonicity condition, along with mild regularity and growth conditions at
infinity. A major novelty of our work is the rigorous treatment of a nontrivial
fixed-point problem on a space of measures, which arises naturally in the MFGC
formulation. Unlike prior works that either restrict to separable Hamiltonians
- rendering the fixed-point map trivial - or assume convergence or regularity
properties of the fixed point map, we develop a detailed structural analysis of
this equation and its N-player analogue. This leads to new regularity results
for the fixed-point maps and, in turn, to quantitative convergence of open-loop
equilibria. We further derive sharp a priori estimates for the N-player Nash
system, enabling us to control the discrepancy between open and closed-loop
strategies, and thus to conclude the convergence of closed-loop equilibria. Our
framework also accommodates common noise in a natural way.

### [47] [Splitting phenomenon in the Sathe-Selberg theorem, mod-Poisson convergence with auxiliary randomisation and universality of the Gamma factor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17072)
*Yacine Barhoumi-Andréani*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了多个随机变量序列的傅里叶-拉普拉斯变换在适当重标度下呈现的分裂现象，解释了通用伽马因子的出现机制，并将理论应用于随机排列、随机高斯整数、有限域上随机多项式等多个数学对象。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过识别各个模型的共同特征——存在揭示独立性结构的辅助随机化过程，利用从属随机变量的概率（指数）波动来解释伽马因子的出现。对多个数学对象（随机排列、随机高斯整数、有限域上的随机多项式和矩阵、随机分割、Sathe-Selberg定理）进行统一分析。

Abstract: We consider several sequences of random variables whose Fourier-Laplace
transforms present the same type of \textit{splitting phenomenon} when suitably
rescaled by the Fourier-Laplace transform of a Poisson-distributed random
variable (mod-Poisson convergence). Addressing a question raised by
Kowalski-Nikeghbali, we explain the appearance of a universal term, the
\textit{Gamma factor}, by a common feature of each model, the existence of an
auxiliary randomisation that reveals an independence structure. This universal
Gamma factor is a consequence of the probabilistic (exponential) fluctuations
of this subordinated random variable.
  The class of examples that belong to this framework includes: random uniform
permutations, random Gauss integers, random polynomials over a finite field,
random matrices with values in a finite field, random partitions and the
classical Sathe-Selberg theorems in probabilistic number theory. For this last
example, the randomisation that triggers the Gamma factor defines a new
probability distribution, the ``delta-Zeta distribution'' which is the analogue
of the geometric distribution in the permutation setting.

Motivation: 双重非线性方程在确定性情况下甚至不具备唯一性，但研究者希望探索随机噪声是否能够带来某种正则化效应，使得随机情况下能够获得更好的数学性质。

Method: 假设加性噪声具有足够的粗糙性，采用Friedrichs型概率弱解的框架来处理双重非线性随机演化方程，通过概率论方法研究解的存在性和法则唯一性。

Result: 成功证明了在粗糙噪声条件下，双重非线性随机演化方程存在Friedrichs型概率弱解，并且这些解在法则意义下具有唯一性。同时建立了随机双重非线性方程近似的弱概率稳定性。

Conclusion: 随机噪声为双重非线性演化方程带来了真正的随机正则化效应，使得原本在确定性情况下不具备唯一性的方程在随机情况下获得了法则唯一性和稳定性，这是一个纯粹的随机现象。

Abstract: Doubly nonlinear stochastic evolution equations are considered. Upon assuming
the additive noise to be rough enough, we prove the existence of
probabilistically weak solutions of Friedrichs type and study their uniqueness
in law. This entails stability for approximations of stochastic doubly
nonlinear equations in a weak probabilistic sense. Such effect is a genuinely
stochastic, as doubly nonlinear equations are not even expected to exhibit
uniqueness in the deterministic case.

</details>


### [51] [A rough path approach to pathwise stochastic integration à la Föllmer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17363)
*Purba Das,Anna P. Kwossek,David J. Prömel*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一个路径随机积分的通用框架，将Föllmer的经典方法扩展到梯度型被积函数和标准左端点黎曼和之外，提供了伊藤积分、Stratonovich积分和后向伊藤积分的路径对应版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Föllmer路径积分方法仅限于梯度型被积函数和标准左端点黎曼和，需要一个更通用的框架来处理更广泛的随机积分类型，包括伊藤积分、Stratonovich积分和后向伊藤积分的路径版本。

Method: 对于沿固定分割序列同时具有二次变分和Lévy面积的连续路径，将路径随机积分定义为一般黎曼和的极限，并证明这些积分与相应粗糙路径定义的积分一致。同时识别连续路径的二次变分和Lévy面积相对于分割序列选择不变的充要条件。

Result: 成功建立了路径随机积分的通用理论框架，证明了所定义的路径积分与粗糙路径积分的等价性，并给出了二次变分和Lévy面积在分割序列变化下保持不变的完整刻画。

Conclusion: 该框架为路径随机积分提供了统一的理论基础，扩展了经典Föllmer方法的适用范围，并建立了与粗糙路径理论的联系，为随机分析提供了新的路径积分工具。

Abstract: We develop a general framework for pathwise stochastic integration that
extends F\"ollmer's classical approach beyond gradient-type integrands and
standard left-point Riemann sums and provides pathwise counterparts of It\^o,
Stratonovich, and backward It\^o integration. More precisely, for a continuous
path admitting both quadratic variation and L\'evy area along a fixed sequence
of partitions, we define pathwise stochastic integrals as limits of general
Riemann sums and prove that they coincide with integrals defined with respect
to suitable rough paths. Furthermore, we identify necessary and sufficient
conditions under which the quadratic variation and the L\'evy area of a
continuous path are invariant with respect to the choice of partition
sequences.

</details>


### [52] [Decoupling the i.i.d. field and the randomisation field in the Curie-Weiss model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17459)
*Yacine Barhoumi-Andréani,Peter Eichelsbacher*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文通过De Finetti表示、拉普拉斯逆变换公式等数学工具，揭示了Curie-Weiss模型的完整相图可以通过De Finetti随机化与复变量索引的近似高斯过程之间的竞争来解释，并将该方法扩展到更广泛的统计力学模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有文献中对Curie-Weiss模型在亚临界和临界情况的结果缺乏统一的解释框架，需要一个能够同时处理所有类型自旋定律的方法，并且能够扩展到包括任意维数Ising模型在内的更广泛统计力学模型类别。

Method: 使用Curie-Weiss模型的De Finetti表示、伯努利随机变量的均匀耦合和拉普拉斯逆变换公式，通过几乎必然的拉普拉斯逆变换方法来分析相图。引入复变量索引的近似高斯过程，该过程等于布朗桥在复直线上的逆拉普拉斯变换，并通过更精细的过程重标度展示这是布朗片的修正。

Result: 成功解释了Curie-Weiss模型的完整相图，表明其可以通过De Finetti随机化与复变量索引高斯过程之间的竞争来理解。在亚临界和临界情况下为已有文献结果提供了自然解释，同时在超临界情况下产生了新的类似结果。证明了该方法可以统一处理所有类型的自旋定律。

Conclusion: 几乎必然拉普拉斯逆变换方法提供了一个统一的框架来理解Curie-Weiss模型的相变行为，该功能性方法可以扩展到包括任意维数Ising模型在内的广泛统计力学模型类别，为统计力学中的相变理论提供了新的数学工具和理论基础。

Abstract: Using the De Finetti representation of the Curie-Weiss model, the uniform
coupling of Bernoulli random variables and the Laplace inversion formula
(almost surely), we show that the full phase diagram of the Curie-Weiss model
can be explained by a competition between the De Finetti randomisation and an
approximate Gaussian process indexed by a complex variable that is equal to the
inverse Laplace transform on a complex line of a Brownian Bridge. A more
refined process type of rescaling shows that this is a modification of the
Brownian Sheet that is at the core of all Gaussian random variables in the
limits obtained in the model. This almost sure Laplace inversion approach
allows moreover to treat all types of spin laws in the same vein as the
Curie-Weiss Bernoulli spins.
  This gives a natural explanation of several results that already appeared in
the literature in the subcritical and critical case in addition to produce new
analogous results in the super-critical case.
  The functional approach here defined can moreover be extended to a wide class
of statistical mechanical models that includes the Ising model in any
dimension.

</details>


### [53] [On the minimal integral energy of majorants of the Wiener process](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17468)
*Sergey Nikitin*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究维纳过程主函数的最小积分能量在长时间区间上的渐近行为，发现动能情况ψ(u)=u²是临界情况，将两种不同的渐近机制分开


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究仅针对动能情况ψ(u)=u²得到了渐近估计，需要将这些结果推广到更一般的积分能量形式，并探索不同能量函数下的渐近行为规律

Method: 考虑维纳过程W(·)的主函数h满足约束条件h(0)=r和h(t)≥W(t)的情况下，分析最小积分能量的渐近行为，通过数学分析方法研究不同ψ函数形式对应的渐近机制

Result: 显著推广了之前仅针对动能情况ψ(u)=u²的渐近估计结果，发现动能情况是一个临界案例，其最小能量呈对数增长，位于两种不同渐近机制之间

Conclusion: 动能情况ψ(u)=u²构成了一个临界分界线，将维纳过程主函数的最小积分能量划分为两种截然不同的渐近增长模式，为理解随机过程约束优化问题提供了新的理论框架

Abstract: We consider the asymptotic behavior (over long time intervals) of the minimal

= r $, $ h(t) \geq W(t) $ for $ 0 \leq t \leq T $. The results significantly
generalize previous asymptotic estimates obtained for the case of kinetic
energy $ \psi(u) = u^2 $, revealing that this case, where the minimal energy
grows logarithmically, is a critical one, lying between two different
asymptotic regimes.

</details>


### [54] [Nonlinear rough Fokker-Planck equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17469)
*Fabio Bugini,Peter K. Friz,Wilhelm Stannat*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文利用粗糙路径技术研究McKean-Vlasov随机微分方程对应的随机Fokker-Planck方程的适定性问题，显著降低了对系数正则性的要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于随机Fokker-Planck方程适定性的最佳结果（Coghi-Gess 2019）需要依赖维数的正则性假设，这是一个困难的问题。需要寻找新的方法来绕过这些限制性的假设条件。

Method: 采用粗糙路径（rough path）技术来研究含有公共噪声和条件律依赖的McKean-Vlasov随机微分方程对应的随机Fokker-Planck方程。

Result: 成功证明了粗糙路径技术可以完全绕过维数依赖的正则性假设，相比于经典随机分析方法，对系数的正则性要求大幅降低。

Conclusion: 粗糙路径方法在处理随机Fokker-Planck方程的适定性问题上具有显著优势，与普遍认知相反，它对系数正则性的要求实际上比传统方法更低，为平均场博弈理论中的重要问题提供了新的解决途径。

Abstract: McKean-Vlasov SDEs describe systems where the dynamics depend on the law of
the process. The corresponding Fokker-Planck equation is a nonlinear, nonlocal
PDE for the corresponding measure flow. In the presence of common noise and
conditional law dependence, the evolution becomes random and is governed by a
stochastic Fokker-Planck equation; that is, a nonlinear, nonlocal SPDE in the
space of measures. (Such equations constitute an important ingredient in the
theory of mean-field games with common noise.) Well-posedness of such SPDEs is
a difficult problem, the best result to date due to Coghi-Gess (2019), which
however comes with dimension-dependent regularity assumptions. In the present
work, we show how rough path techniques can circumvent these entirely. Hence,
and somewhat contrarily to common believe, the use of rough paths leads to
substantially less regularity demands on the coefficients than methods rooted
in classical stochastic analysis methods.

</details>

### [57] [The smallest singular value of sparse discrete random matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17741)
*Kexin Yu*

Main category: math.PR

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Spielman-Teng定理需要扩展到稀疏离散随机矩阵的情况，特别是处理具有μ-lazy随机变量元素的矩阵，以推广Tao和Vu之前的工作

Result: 证明了近似Spielman-Teng定理：存在常数C,c>0使得对所有η≥0，有P(sn(Mn)≤η)≲nCη+exp(-nc)，并成功应用于μ-lazy随机变量的情况

Conclusion: 成功建立了稀疏离散随机矩阵的近似Spielman-Teng定理框架，扩展了现有理论到μ-lazy随机变量情况，为随机矩阵理论提供了新的工具和结果

Abstract: Let $M_n$ be an $n \times n$ random matrix with i.i.d. sparse discrete
entries. In this paper, we develop a simple framework to solve the approximate
Spielman-Teng theorem for $M_n$, which has the following form: There exist
constants $C, c>0$ such that for all $\eta \geq 0$,
$\textbf{P}\left(s_n\left(M_n\right) \leq \eta\right) \lesssim n^C \eta+\exp
\left(-n^c\right)$. As an application, we give an approximate Spielman-Teng
theorem for $M_n$ whose entries are $\mu-$lazy random variables, extending
previous work by Tao and Vu.

</details>

Motivation: 研究Siegel模形式的唯一性问题，特别是探索向量值genus 3 Siegel尖形式是否可由其Fourier系数的子集唯一确定

Result: 成功证明了对于奇数且无平方因子的N，具有特定nebentypus的$\Gamma_0^3(N)$向量值genus 3 Siegel尖形式由其基本Fourier系数唯一确定；加强了genus 2的对应结果；证明了基本指标Jacobi形式的判别式性质

Conclusion: 建立了Siegel模形式唯一性确定的新理论结果，从genus 2推广到genus 3，为模形式理论提供了重要的理论贡献，特别是在Fourier系数确定性方面的深入理解

Abstract: We prove that vector-valued genus 3 Siegel cusp forms for $\Gamma_0^3(N)$
with certain nebentypus are determined by their fundamental Fourier
coefficients, assuming $N$ is odd and square-free. A key step in our proof
involves strengthening the known corresponding genus 2 result. More precisely,
we show that genus 2 Siegel cusp forms for $\Gamma_0^2(N)$ with certain
nebentypus are determined by their fundamental Fourier coefficients whose
discriminants are coprime to $N$. We also prove that Jacobi forms of
fundamental index with discriminant coprime to the odd level $N$ are determined
by their primitive theta components.

</details>


### [62] [Monogenic sextic trinomials $x^6+Ax^3+B$ and their Galois groups](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17021)
*Joshua Harrington,Lenny Jones*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文研究形如 $f(x)=x^6+Ax^3+B$ 的不可约三项式在有理数域上的单生成性质，并针对每种可能的伽罗瓦群给出了明确的单生成三项式描述

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究六次三项式 $f(x)=x^6+Ax^3+B$ 何时为单生成的（monogenic），即其根 $\theta$ 的幂次 $\{1,\theta,\theta^2,\theta^3,\theta^4,\theta^{5}\}$ 构成数域 ${\mathbb Q}(\theta)$ 整数环的基

Method: 使用 Jakhar, Khanduja 和 Sangwan 的定理，针对 $f(x)$ 在有理数域上的每种可能伽罗瓦群 $G$，给出所有具有伽罗瓦群 $G$ 的单生成三项式的明确描述

Result: 对于六次不可约三项式的每种可能伽罗瓦群，都给出了相应单生成三项式的明确刻画，并研究了这些三项式何时生成不同的六次数域

Conclusion: 完整地刻画了形如 $x^6+Ax^3+B$ 的单生成三项式，并按伽罗瓦群进行了分类，同时分析了它们生成不同六次数域的条件

Abstract: Let $f(x)=x^6+Ax^3+B\in {\mathbb Z}[x]$, with $A\ne 0$, and suppose that

  For each possible Galois group $G$ of $f(x)$ over ${\mathbb Q}$, we use a

### [63] [Twisted periods of modular forms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17041)
*Tianyu Ni,Hui Xue*

Main category: math.NT

TL;DR: 本文研究了权重为k、水平为1的尖点形式空间中的扭转周期，证明了在k足够大时，具有相同扭转但不同指标的周期线性无关，以及具有相同指标但不同扭转的周期线性无关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究模形式理论中扭转周期的线性无关性质，这对理解L函数的中心值和除数函数的卷积和具有重要意义。扭转周期在数论和模形式理论中是基础概念，其线性无关性直接关系到相关数学对象的非平凡性质。

Method: 通过研究带有nebentypus的水平D的Eisenstein级数的乘积和Rankin-Cohen括号的迹来实现主要结果。具体方法包括：1) 引入扭转周期r_{t,χ}的定义；2) 分析这些周期在不同参数下的线性关系；3) 利用Eisenstein级数的性质建立线性无关性的判定条件。

Result: 证明了两个主要的线性无关性定理：当k相对于n和D足够大时，任意n个具有相同扭转但不同指标的周期线性无关；当k相对于D足够大时，任意n个具有相同指标但不同模D扭转的周期线性无关。此外，还给出了两个应用：证明了扭转除数函数卷积和的恒等式，以及证明Maeda猜想蕴含标准化Hecke特征形式的扭转中心L值的非零性结果。

Conclusion: 本文成功建立了尖点形式空间中扭转周期的线性无关性理论，为模形式理论提供了新的工具和视角。这些结果不仅在理论上具有重要意义，还在除数函数恒等式和L函数中心值研究等具体应用中展现了价值，为相关数论问题的研究开辟了新的途径。

Abstract: Let $S_k$ denote the space of cusp forms of weight $k$ and level one. For
$0\leq t\leq k-2$ and primitive Dirichlet character $\chi$ mod $D$, we
introduce twisted periods $r_{t,\chi}$ on $S_k$. We show that for a fixed
natural number $n$, if $k$ is sufficiently large relative to $n$ and $D$, then
any $n$ periods with the same twist but different indices are linearly
independent. We also prove that if $k$ is sufficiently large relative to $D$
then any $n$ periods with the same index but different twists mod $D$ are
linearly independent. These results are achieved by studying the trace of the
products and Rankin-Cohen brackets of Eisenstein series of level $D$ with
nebentypus. Moreover, we give two applications of our method. First, we prove
certain identities that evaluate convolution sums of twisted divisor functions.
Second, we show that Maeda's conjecture implies a non-vanishing result on
twisted central $L$-values of normalized Hecke eigenforms.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 成功建立了带有棱镜F-晶体系数的de Rham上同调与晶体上同调之间的比较定理，这是对经典Berthelot-Ogus定理的推广和改进。

Conclusion: 通过棱镜上同调的栈理论视角，不仅推广了经典的上同调比较定理，还为理解de Rham上同调和晶体上同调中扭转元素之间的关系提供了新的积分性工具和方法。

tensoring with $K$. In this article, we use the stacky perspective on prismatic
cohomology, due to Drinfeld and Bhatt--Lurie, to give a version of this
comparison result with coefficients in a perfect complex of prismatic
$F$-crystals on $X$. Our method is of an integral nature and suggests new tools

cohomology.

### [72] [On tested Bousfield-Friedlander localizations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17321)
*Niall Taggart*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Bousfield-Friedlander局部化的不同表征方式，特别是探索如何通过左Bousfield局部化来理解带有测试态射集的Bousfield-Friedlander局部化，以及建立相应的齐次模型结构理论。

Method: 采用范畴论和同伦论的方法，通过证明带有测试态射集的Bousfield-Friedlander局部化与左Bousfield局部化的等价性，建立齐次模型结构，并通过具体的微积分理论（离散微积分、Goodwillie微积分、Weiss微积分）来验证和应用这一理论框架。

Result: 证明了测试Bousfield-Friedlander局部化的新表征定理；建立了相关的齐次模型结构；证明了离散微积分与Goodwillie微积分中齐次函子的同伦等价性；证明了Weiss微积分的多项式模型结构是测试Bousfield-Friedlander局部化的一个特例。

Conclusion: 研究成功建立了测试Bousfield-Friedlander局部化的新理论框架，通过左Bousfield局部化的观点提供了更深入的理解，并在具体的微积分理论中验证了这一框架的有效性，为相关领域的进一步研究提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We demonstrate that a Bousfield-Friedlander localization with a set of test
morphisms in the sense introduced by Bandklayder, Bergner, Griffiths, Johnson,
and Santhanam can also be characterized as a left Bousfield localization at the
set of test morphisms. This viewpoint enables us to establish a homogeneous
model structure associated with any calculus arising from a
Bousfield-Friedlander localization of this form. As a corollary, we show that
homogeneous functors in discrete calculus coincide up to homotopy with those in
Goodwillie calculus. Finally, we illustrate this framework by proving that the
polynomial model structure of Weiss calculus is a particular instance of tested
Bousfield-Friedlander localization.

### [73] [Obstruction theory for $A$-infinity bimodules](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17568)
*Gustavo Jasso,Fernando Muro*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文为截断极小A∞双模结构在截断极小A∞代数上的扩展建立了阻碍理论，利用Bousfield-Kan型谱序列来刻画阻碍，并引入了新的上同调理论来描述谱序列的第二页。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的A∞代数和双模理论缺乏对截断情况下扩展问题的系统性阻碍理论，特别是在处理极小A∞双模结构扩展时遇到的技术障碍，需要新的上同调工具和谱序列方法来解决。

Method: 构造Bousfield-Kan型的截断带边谱序列，其阻碍位于远处页面；引入与分次代数和分次双模对相关的新上同调理论；利用Gerstenhaber括号和双模类似的通用Massey乘积描述谱序列的第二微分；建立d-稀疏情况的变体理论。

Result: 建立了截断极小A∞双模结构扩展的完整阻碍理论；新上同调理论与Hochschild上同调和双模自扩张形成长正合序列；证明了微分分次双模在微分分次代数上的内在形式性和几乎形式性定理；理论推广到带乘法的分次操作子情况。

Conclusion: 成功建立了截断极小A∞双模扩展的阻碍理论框架，为理解A∞结构的变形和扩展提供了新的工具，特别是在微分分次代数几何和同伦代数理论中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: We develop an obstruction theory for the extension of truncated minimal
$A$-infinity bimodule structures over truncated minimal $A$-infinity algebras.
Obstructions live in far-away pages of a (truncated) fringed spectral sequence
of Bousfield--Kan type. The second page of this spectral sequence is mostly
given by a new cohomology theory associated to a pair consisting of a graded
algebra and a graded bimodule over it. This new cohomology theory fits in a
long exact sequence involving the Hochschild cohomology of the algebra and the
self-extensions of the bimodule. We show that the second differential of this
spectral sequence is given by the Gerstenhaber bracket with a bimodule analogue
of the universal Massey product of a minimal $A$-infinity algebra. We also
develop a closely-related obstruction theory for truncated minimal $A$-infinity
bimodule structures over (the truncation of) a fixed minimal $A$-infinity
algebra; the second page of the corresponding spectral sequence is now mostly
given by the vector spaces of self-extensions of the underlying graded bimodule
and the second differential is described analogously to the previous one. We
also establish variants of the above for graded algebras and graded bimodules
that are $d$-sparse, that is they are concentrated in degrees that are
multiples of a fixed integer $d\geq1$. These obstruction theories are used to
establish intrinsic formality and almost formality theorems for differential
graded bimodules over differential graded algebras. Our results hold, more
generally, in the context of graded operads with multiplication equipped with
an associative operadic ideal, examples of which are the endomorphism operad of
a graded algebra and the linear endomorphism operad of a pair consisting of a
graded algebra and a graded bimodule over it.

</details>


### [74] [Spaces of homomorphisms, formality and Hochschild homology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17683)
*Simon Gritschacher*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文研究离散群的有限维酉表示的拓扑范畴，证明了对于有限生成群G和阿贝尔群A，存在E∞-空间的分解定理，并应用此结果研究同态簇的同调稳定性和等变同调性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究离散群的有限维酉表示范畴的拓扑性质，特别是当群为直积形式时的结构分解，以及由此导出的同态簇的同调稳定性问题。

Method: 利用对称单调范畴理论和E∞-空间的张量积分解，结合Kupers-Miller的局部到全局同调稳定性原理，以及高阶Hochschild同调理论来分析表示范畴的拓扑结构。

Result: 证明了K^def(G×A)≃K^def(G)⊗Â作为E∞-空间的同构，建立了同态簇Hom(G×Z^r,U(n))的同调稳定性，并描述了自由群情况下的等变同调结构，特别计算了Hom(F×Z^r,U(2))的Poincaré多项式。

Conclusion: 通过E∞-空间的张量积分解定理，成功将复杂的群表示问题转化为更易处理的组件，为研究同态簇的拓扑性质提供了有效的工具和具体的计算结果。

Abstract: Let $G$ be a discrete group. The topological category of finite dimensional
unitary representations of $G$ is symmetric monoidal under direct sum and has
an associated $\mathbb{E}_\infty$-space $\mathcal{K}^{\mathrm{def}}(G)$. We
show that if $G$ and $A$ are finitely generated groups and $A$ is abelian, then
$\mathcal{K}^{\mathrm{def}}(G\times A)\simeq
\mathcal{K}^{\mathrm{def}}(G)\otimes \widehat{A}$ as
$\mathbb{E}_\infty$-spaces, where $\widehat{A}$ is the Pontryagin dual of $A$.
We deduce a homology stability result for the homomorphism varieties
$\mathrm{Hom}(G\times \mathbb{Z}^r,U(n))$ using the local-to-global principle
for homology stability of Kupers--Miller. For a finitely generated free group
$F$ and a field $k$ of characteristic zero, we show that the singular
$k$-chains in $\mathcal{K}^{\mathrm{def}}(F)$ are formal as an
$\mathbb{E}_\infty$-$k$-algebra. Using this we describe the equivariant
homology of $\mathrm{Hom}(F \times A,U(n))$ for every $n$ in terms of higher
Hochschild homology of an explicitly determined commutative $k$-algebra. As an
example we show that $\mathrm{Hom}(F\times \mathbb{Z}^r,U(2))$ is
$U(2)$-equivariantly formal for every $r$ and we compute the Poincar{\'e}
polynomial.

</details>

### [77] [Planar-Toroidal Decomposition of $K_{12}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17084)
*Allan Bickle,Russell Campbell*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 该论文通过理论分析和计算机搜索证明了完全图K₁₂无法分解为一个平面图和一个环面图，并找到了所有使得平面图的补图中环面子图边数达到最大值的图对。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1978年Anderson和White提出了一个问题：是否存在将完全图K₁₂分解为一个平面图和一个环面图的方法。这是图论中关于图分解的一个重要问题，涉及平面图和环面图的性质研究。

Method: 采用理论论证结合计算机搜索的方法。首先通过理论分析建立相关性质，然后对所有12阶最大平面图进行穷举计算机搜索，验证理论结果并寻找满足特定条件的图对。

Result: 证明了K₁₂不存在分解为一个平面图和一个环面图的方案。进一步证明了如果G是12阶平面图，H是G的补图的环面子图，则H的边数至少比G的补图少2条边。通过计算机搜索找到了123个唯一的图对(G,H)使得这个不等式取等号。

Conclusion: Anderson和White在1978年提出的问题得到了否定的答案：K₁₂无法分解为一个平面图和一个环面图。同时建立了12阶平面图补图中环面子图边数的上界，并完整枚举了达到这个上界的所有情况。

Abstract: In 1978, Anderson and White asked whether there is a decomposition of
$K_{12}$ into two graphs, one planar and one toroidal. Using theoretical
arguments and a computer search of all maximal planar graphs of order 12, we
show that no such decomposition exists. We further show that if $G$ is planar
of order 12 and $H\subseteq\overline{G}$ is toroidal, then $H$ has at least two
fewer edges than $\overline{G}$. A computer search found all 123 unique pairs
$\left(G,H\right)$ that make this an equality.

### [78] [Resolving Open Problems on the Euler Sombor Index](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17246)
*Kinkar Chandra Das,Jayanta Bera*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文完全解决了Euler Sombor指数相关的两个具有挑战性的开放问题：确定了固定阶数和围长的单环图中EUS指数的最小值及其极值图，并分类了固定阶数和叶子数的连通图中达到最大EUS指数的所有图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Khanra和Das最近提出了关于Euler Sombor指数的几个开放问题，这些问题在图论和化学图理论中具有重要意义。本文旨在完全解决其中最具挑战性的两个问题。

Method: 通过数学分析和图论技术，系统研究Euler Sombor指数在不同图类中的极值性质。首先分析单环图的情况，然后扩展到更广泛的连通图类，最后研究固定参数下的最大值问题。

Result: 1) 确定了固定阶数和围长的单环图中EUS指数的最小值，并刻画了达到此最小值的极值图；2) 建立了相同阶数和围长的连通图中EUS指数的最小值，并识别了相应的极值结构；3) 完全分类了在固定阶数和叶子数条件下达到最大Euler Sombor指数的所有连通图。

Conclusion: 本文成功解决了Euler Sombor指数研究中的两个重要开放问题，为该拓扑指数的理论发展做出了重要贡献，同时为化学图理论和分子结构分析提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Recently, the Euler Sombor index $(EUS)$ was introduced as a novel
degree-based topological index. For a graph $G$, the Euler Sombor index is
defined as $$EUS(G) = \sum_{v_i v_j \in E(G)} \sqrt{d_i^2 + d_j^2 + d_i d_j},$$
where $d_i$ and $d_j$ denote the degrees of the vertices $v_i$ and $v_j$,
respectively. Very recently, Khanra and Das \textbf{\bf [Euler Sombor index of
trees, unicyclic and chemical graphs, \emph{MATCH Commun. Math. Comput. Chem.}
\textbf{94} (2025) 525--548]} proposed several open problems concerning the
Euler Sombor index. This paper completely resolves two of the most challenging
problems posed therein. First, we determine the minimum value of the $EUS$
index among all unicyclic graphs of a fixed order and prescribed girth, and we
characterize the extremal graphs that attain this minimum. Building on this
result, we further establish the minimum $EUS$ index within the broader class
of connected graphs of the same order and girth, and identify the corresponding
extremal structures. In addition, we classify all connected graphs that attain
the maximum Euler Sombor index $(EUS)$ when both the order and the number of
leaves are fixed.

### [79] [Bipartite graphs with minimum degree at least 15 are antimagic](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17302)
*Kecai Deng*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文证明了最小度至少为15的二部图都是反魔术的，为反魔术标记猜想提供了新的进展


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 反魔术标记猜想（Hartsfield和Ringel在1990年提出）声称除了K₂之外的每个连通图都是反魔术的。之前的研究仅对平均度至少为4,182的图证明了该猜想，且无法将界限降低到1,000以下。需要新的方法来处理度数更小的特殊图类

Method: 采用三个主要工具：1）Koenig定理的推论；2）存在特定大小且避免欧拉分量的子图；3）标记引理，确保某些顶点和能被3整除而其他不能

Result: 成功证明了最小度至少为15的所有二部图都是反魔术的，这显著改进了之前需要平均度至少4,182的结果

Conclusion: 通过专门针对二部图的新方法，大幅降低了反魔术标记猜想成立所需的度数条件，从平均度4,182降低到最小度15，为该重要猜想提供了实质性进展

Abstract: An antimagic {labeling} of a graph $G=(V,E)$ is a one-to-one mapping $f:
E\rightarrow\{1,2,\ldots,|E|\}$, ensuring that the vertex sums in $V$ are
pairwise distinct, where a vertex sum of a vertex $v$ is defined as the sum of
the labels of the edges incident to $v$. A graph is called antimagic if it
admits an antimagic labeling. The Antimagic Labeling Conjecture, proposed by
Hartsfield and Ringel in 1990, posits that every connected graph other than
$K_2$ is antimagic. The conjecture was confirmed for graphs of average degree
at least 4,182 in 2016 by Eccles, where it was stated that a similar approach
could not reduce the bound below 1,000 from 4,182.
  This paper shows that every bipartite graph with minimum degree at least 15
is antimagic. Our approach relies on three tools: a consequence of K\"{o}nig's
Theorem, the existence of a subgraph of a specific size that avoids Eulerian
components, and a labeling lemma that ensures some vertex sums are divisible by
three while others are not.

</details>

Abstract: The Maker-Breaker total domination number, $\gamma_{\rm MBT}(G)$, of a graph
$G$ is introduced as the minimum number of moves of Dominator to win the
Maker-Breaker total domination game, provided that he has a winning strategy
and is the first to play. The Staller-start Maker-Breaker total domination

exists a connected graph $G$ with $\gamma_{\rm MB}(G)=k$ and $\gamma_{\rm

MB}'(G')=k$ and $\gamma_{\rm MBT}'(G')=\ell$, and (iii) there there exists a
connected graph $G''$ with $\gamma_{\rm MBT}(G'')=k$ and $\gamma_{\rm
MBT}'(G'')=\ell$. Here, $\gamma_{\rm MB}$ and $\gamma_{\rm MB}'$ are
corresponding invariants for the Maker-Breaker domination game.

### [81] [Clustering, order conditions, and languages of interval exchanges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17370)
*Sébastien Ferenczi,Luca Q. Zamboni*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究区间交换变换（标准和广义）的自然编码特性，特别是探索Burrows-Wheeler变换聚类性质与诱导映射之间的关系，以及广义区间交换变换与标准区间交换变换的联系。

Method: 定义从字母集合到回归词集合的态射φ，保持字典序；分析词w的聚类性质与诱导映射T在柱面[w]上的聚类性质之间的关系；利用对称性质和回文特性研究自然编码的丰富语言特性。

Result: 证明了词φv对变换T的置换聚类当且仅当词v对T在柱面[w]上诱导映射的置换聚类；当T是对称的且w是回文时，相关的两个序是相同的；将已知的聚类词ww的结果推广到非聚类情况。

Conclusion: 在对称情况下，证明了词w由广义区间交换变换产生当且仅当w由标准区间交换变换产生，这个结果不依赖于聚类性质，是对之前聚类情况下类似结论的重要推广。

Abstract: For any interval exchange transformation $T$ (standard or generalized), if we
define a morphism $\phi$ from the set of letters to the
  set of the return words of a word in the natural coding, respecting the
lexicographical order, the word $\phi v$ clusters (for the Burrows-Wheeler
transform) for the permutation of $T$ if and only if the word $v$ clusters for
the permutation of the induced map of $T$
  on the cylinder $[w]$. When $T$ is symmetrical, all such natural codings are
rich languages, and this implies that the two orders above are the same if $w$
is a palindrome. Finally, we generalize the result, proved by using the
clustering of a word $w$,
  that $ww$ is produced by a generalized interval exchange transformation if
and only if $ww$ is produced by a standard interval exchange transformation, to
non-clustering $w$: in the symmetric case, $w$ is produced by a
  generalized interval exchange transformation if and only if $w$ is produced
by a standard interval exchange transformation.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明对于每个正整数d，都存在代数度为d的循环图，但缺乏对最小阶数C(d)的精确计算和对d-积分循环图数量的系统分析。需要找到具有给定代数度的最小循环图，并研究此类图的唯一性问题。

Method: 通过分析循环图的邻接多项式在有理数域上的分裂域维数来定义代数度，引入最小d-积分循环图的概念，使用代数数论和图论方法来计算C(d)的精确值，并通过组合分析来估计同构类数量|𝒻_{n,d}|的界限。

Result: 成功计算出了C(d)的精确值，证明了最小d-积分循环图不是唯一的，给出了|𝒻_{n,d}|的界限估计，并在p和d都为素数的特殊情况下得到了|𝒻_{p,d}|的精确值。

Conclusion: 本研究完整解决了最小d-积分循环图的阶数问题，揭示了此类图的非唯一性，为循环图代数度理论提供了重要的定量结果，特别是在素数情况下给出了完整的分类。

Abstract: The algebraic degree $Deg(G)$ of a graph $G$ is the dimension of the
splitting field of the adjacency polynomial of $G$ over the field $\mathbb{Q}$.
It can be shown that for every positive integer $d$, there exists a circulant
graph with algebraic degree $d$. Let $C(d)$ be the least positive integer such
that there exists a circulant graph of order $C(d)$ having algebraic degree
$d$. A graph $G$ is called $d$-integral if $Deg(G)=d$. We call a $d$-integral
circulant graph \textit{minimal} if order of that graph equals $C(d)$. Let
$\mathcal{F}_{n,d}$ denote the collection of isomorphism classes of connected,
$d$-integral circulant graphs of some given possible order $n$. In this paper
we compute the exact value of $C(d)$ and provide some bounds on
$|\mathcal{F}_{n,d}|$, thereby showing that the minimal $d$-integral circulant
graph is not unique. Moreover, we find the exact value of $|\mathcal{F}_{p,d}|$
where both $p$ and $d$ are prime.

</details>


### [83] [On the sum of the largest and smallest eigenvalues of odd-cycle free graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17492)
*Aida Abiad,Vladislav Taranchuk,Thijs van Veluw*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文将Csikvári关于奇围长为5的图的特征值界限结果推广到一般奇围长k的图，证明了$(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n = O(k^{-1})$，并给出奇围长为7时的更强上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 图的二部性可以通过邻接矩阵的最大和最小特征值之和$\lambda_1 + \lambda_n$以及奇围长来衡量。Csikvári在2022年证明了对于奇围长为5的无三角形图有$(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n \le (3-2\sqrt 2) < 0.1716$。本文希望将这一结果推广到更一般的奇围长情况。

Method: 本文采用特征值分析方法，通过研究图的邻接矩阵特征值与图的结构性质（特别是奇围长）之间的关系，利用数学分析技巧来建立特征值界限与奇围长之间的定量关系。

Result: 1. 证明了对于一般奇围长为k的图，有$(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n = O(k^{-1})$的渐近界限；2. 对于奇围长为7的特殊情况，给出了更精确的上界$(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n < 0.0396$，这比一般性结果更强。

Conclusion: 本文成功将Csikvári的结果从奇围长5推广到任意奇围长k，建立了特征值界限与奇围长之间的反比关系，并在奇围长7的情况下给出了改进的数值界限，为理解图的二部性提供了新的理论工具。

Abstract: Let $G$ be a graph with adjacency eigenvalues $\lambda_1 \geq \cdots \geq
\lambda_n$. Both $\lambda_1 + \lambda_n$ and the odd girth of $G$ can be seen
as measures of the bipartiteness of $G$. Csikv\'ari proved in 2022 that for odd
girth 5 graphs (triangle-free) it holds that $(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n \le
(3-2\sqrt 2) < 0.1716$. In this paper we extend Csikv\'ari's result to general
odd girth $k$ proving that $(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n = O(k^{-1})$. In the case
of odd girth 7, we prove a stronger upper bound of $(\lambda_1+\lambda_n)/n <
0.0396$.

</details>


### [84] [Approximating temporal modularity on graphs of small underlying treewidth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17541)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 模块度是衡量网络聚类或社区结构的重要指标，但在时序图（边集随时间变化的图）上计算模块度极其困难，是NP-hard问题。现有算法只在非常受限的特殊情况下有效，因此需要开发新的高效算法来处理更现实的时序网络模型。

Method: 将静态图模块度的乘性近似算法推广到时序图情况，针对底层图具有小树宽的情况设计算法。开发了新的技术思路来克服时序问题带来的技术挑战，使得算法能够高效处理时序图的模块度计算。

Result: 成功设计出了一个能够在小树宽时序图上高效计算时序模块度乘性近似的算法。该算法扩展了静态情况下的类似近似算法，并有效解决了时序特性带来的技术难题。

Conclusion: 证明了当底层图具有小树宽时，可以高效计算时序模块度的乘性近似。这一结果为处理现实世界中连接随时间演化的网络（如社交网络）提供了重要的理论基础和算法工具，是静态情况算法的重要推广。

Abstract: Modularity is a very widely used measure of the level of clustering or
community structure in networks. Here we consider a recent generalisation of
the definition of modularity to temporal graphs, whose edge-sets change over
discrete timesteps; such graphs offer a more realistic model of many real-world
networks in which connections between entities (for example, between
individuals in a social network) evolve over time. Computing modularity is
notoriously difficult: it is NP-hard even to approximate in general, and only
admits efficient exact algorithms in very restricted special cases. Our main
result is that a multiplicative approximation to temporal modularity can be
computed efficiently when the underlying graph has small treewidth. This
generalises a similar approximation algorithm for the static case, but requires
some substantially new ideas to overcome technical challenges associated with
the temporal nature of the problem.

Method: 引入可扩展凸性的新概念来描述嵌入投影簇中实半代数集的凸性；构造外循环多面体作为amplituhedron在Plücker嵌入下的凸包；通过组合分析研究外循环多面体的面和对偶；定义可扩展对偶amplituhedron并分析其性质

Abstract: The amplituhedron is a semialgebraic set in the Grassmannian. We study
convexity and duality of amplituhedra. We introduce a notion of convexity,
called \textit{extendable convexity}, for real semialgebraic sets in any
embedded projective variety. We show that the $k=m=2$ amplituhedron is
extendably convex in the Grassmannian of lines in projective three-space. In
the process we introduce a new polytope called the \emph{exterior cyclic
polytope}, generalizing the cyclic polytope. It is equal to the convex hull of
the amplituhedron in the Pl\"ucker embedding. We undertake a combinatorial
analysis of the exterior cyclic polytope, its facets, and its dual. Finally, we
introduce the \textit{(extendable) dual amplituhedron}, which is closely
related to the dual of the exterior cyclic polytope. We show that the dual
amplituhedron for $k=m=2$ is again an amplituhedron, where the external matrix
data is changed by the twist map.

Abstract: The Maker-Breaker domination game is played on a graph $G$ by Dominator and
Staller who alternate turns selecting an unplayed vertex of $G$. The goal of
Dominator is that the vertices he selected during the game form a dominating
set while Staller's goal is to prevent this from happening. The graph invariant
$\gamma_{\rm MB}'(G)$ is the number of Dominator's moves in the game played on
$G$ in which he can achieve his goal when Staller makes the first move and both
players play optimally. In this paper, we continue the investigation of
$2$-$\gamma_{\rm MB}'$-critical graphs, initiated in [Divarakan et al.,
Maker--Breaker domination game critical graphs, Discrete Appl.\ Math. 368
(2025) 126--134], which are defined as the graphs $G$ with $\gamma_{\rm
MB}'(G)=2$ and $\gamma_{\rm MB}'(G-e)>2$ for every edge $e$ in $G$. The authors
characterized bipartite $2$-$\gamma_{\rm MB}'$-critical graphs, and found an
example of a non-bipartite $2$-$\gamma_{\rm MB}'$-critical graph. In this
paper, we characterize the $2$-$\gamma_{\rm MB}'$-critical graphs that have a
cut-vertex, which are represented by two infinite families. In addition, we
prove that $C_5$ is the only non-bipartite, triangle-free $2$-$\gamma_{\rm
MB}'$-critical graph.

### [89] [Optimal stability results on color-biased Hamilton cycles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17739)
*Wenchong Chen,Mingyuan Rong,Zixiang Xu*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究边着色图中的哈密顿环，重点关注颜色偏差（色彩频率偏离均匀分布的最大程度）。证明了当最小度超过特定阈值但所有哈密顿环的颜色偏差都很小时，图的结构必须接近已知的极值构造。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究确定了保证存在具有一定颜色偏差的哈密顿环所需的最小度条件，并刻画了极值图的结构。然而，缺乏对结构稳定性的深入理解，即当图接近但未达到极值条件时的结构特征。

Method: 利用局部配置来推断全局结构，建立严格的组合二分法。通过分析当最小度条件略有放松但仍保持较强约束时，图必须保持的结构性质。使用概率方法和极值图论技术来证明结构稳定性结果。

Result: 证明了最优的稳定性结果：对于r≥2和m<2^(-6)r²n，如果n顶点图的最小度超过n/2+6r²m，且每个哈密顿环的颜色偏差都小于m，则该图必须接近Freschi等人的极值构造。证明了度条件中的主导项n/2是最优的，附加误差项Θ(m)在m较大且r=2时也是最优的。

Conclusion: 结构稳定性阈值1/2严格低于强制颜色不平衡所需的极值阈值1/2+1/(2r)，这揭示了边着色哈密顿环问题中的精细结构。该结果为理解接近极值条件时图的结构提供了深入洞察。

Abstract: We investigate Hamilton cycles in edge-colored graphs with \( r \) colors,
focusing on the notion of color-bias (discrepancy), the maximum deviation from
uniform color frequencies along a cycle. Foundational work by Balogh, Csaba,
Jing, and Pluh\'{a}r, and the later generalization by Freschi, Hyde, Lada, and
Treglown, as well as an independent work by Gishboliner, Krivelevich, and
Michaeli, established that any \(n\)-vertex graph with minimum degree exceeding
\( \frac{(r+1)n}{2r} + \frac{m}{2}\) contains a Hamilton cycle with color-bias
at least \(m\), and characterized the extremal graphs with minimum degree
\(\frac{(r+1)n}{2r}\) in which all Hamilton cycles are perfectly balanced.
  We prove the optimal stability results: for any positive integers \(r\ge 2\)
and \( m < 2^{-6} r^{2} n,\) if every Hamilton cycle in an \( n \)-vertex graph
with minimum degree exceeding \( \frac{n}{2} + 6r^{2}m \) has color-bias less
than \( m \), then the graph must closely resemble the extremal constructions
of Freschi, Hyde, Lada, and Treglown. The leading term \( \frac{n}{2} \) in the
degree condition is optimal, as it is the sharp threshold for guaranteeing
Hamiltonicity. Moreover, we show the additive error term \(\Theta(m)\) is also
best possible when \(m\) is large and \(r=2\), since weaker condition
$\frac{n}{2}+o(m)$ allow for a counterexample. Notably, the structural
stability threshold \( \frac{1}{2} \) lies strictly below the extremal
threshold \( \frac{1}{2} + \frac{1}{2r} \) required to force color imbalance.
Our proof leverages local configurations to deduce global structure, revealing
a rigid combinatorial dichotomy.

</details>
