### [90] [On local rings of finite syzygy representation type](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17097)
*Souvik Dey,Kaito Kimura,Jian Liu,Yuya Otake*

Main category: math.AC

TL;DR: 本文研究交换诺特局部环的完备化的孤立奇点刻画问题，改进了多个已有定理，解决了Schreyer猜想，并探讨了Cohen-Macaulay表示型和Gorenstein投射模的相关问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于交换诺特局部环完备化孤立奇点的刻画定理存在改进空间，同时Schreyer猜想尚未得到完全解决，Chen问题在Cohen-Macaulay环上的类似问题也需要进一步研究。

Method: 通过研究有限和可数syzygy表示型在从环R到其完备化的标准映射下的上升和下降性质，利用Cohen-Macaulay环上的表示理论和Gorenstein投射模理论进行分析。

Result: 给出了交换诺特局部环完备化具有孤立奇点的完整刻画；完全肯定地回答了Schreyer猜想；证明了在一定条件下Cohen-Macaulay环要么是超曲面要么每个Gorenstein投射模都是投射的；识别了一类新的虚拟Gorenstein环。

Conclusion: 本文的结果不仅改进了Dao-Takahashi等人的多个重要定理，还解决了Schreyer猜想这一重要问题，为交换代数中的表示理论和奇点理论提供了新的深入理解，特别是在Cohen-Macaulay环和Gorenstein投射模方面取得了重要进展。

Abstract: Let R be a commutative Noetherian local ring. We give a characterization of
when the completion of R has an isolated singularity. This result
simultaneously improves a theorem of Dao and Takahashi and a theorem of
Bahlekeh, Hakimian, Salarian, and Takahashi. As an application, we strengthen
the Auslander-Huneke-Leuschke-Wiegand theorem in the form refined by Dao and
Takahashi. We further investigate the ascent and descent of finite and
countable syzygy representation type along the canonical map from R to its
completion. As a consequence, we obtain a complete affirmative answer to
Schreyer's conjecture. We also explore analogues of Chen's questions in the
context of finite Cohen-Macaulay representation type over Cohen-Macaulay rings.
The main result in this direction shows that if R is Cohen-Macaulay and there
are only finitely many non-isomorphic indecomposable maximal Cohen-Macaulay
modules that are locally free on the punctured spectrum, then either R is a
hypersurface or every Gorenstein projective module is projective, and every
Gorenstein projective module over the completion of R is a direct sum of
finitely generated ones. Finally, we study dominant local rings, introduced by
Takahashi, under certain finite representation type conditions, and identify a
new class of virtually Gorenstein rings.

</details>

Abstract: In this survey we collect some recent advances concerning embedding theorems

reseach area will also be discusssed shortly and posed by us. The paper

### [94] [On Hopf's conjecture and positive second intermediate Ricci curvature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16936)
*Lee Kennard,Lawrence Mouillé,Jan Nienhaus*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文研究了具有正第二中间里奇曲率的流形在特定条件下的欧拉特征问题，证明了在维数被4整除且环面对称秩至少为10的情况下，这类流形具有正欧拉特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Hopf猜想指出偶维闭黎曼流形若具有正截面曲率则有正欧拉特征，但当将正截面曲率条件放宽为正第二中间里奇曲率时，该结论不再成立。因此需要寻找在放宽曲率条件下仍能保证正欧拉特征的额外条件。

Method: 主要方法是将第一作者的四周期性定理进行非平凡扩展，使其适用于上同调的周期性不能延伸到零次的情况。结合环面对称性的几何分析来研究流形的拓扑性质。

Result: 证明了如果一个具有正第二中间里奇曲率的流形其维数被4整除且具有秩至少为10的环面对称性，那么它具有正欧拉特征。这为Hopf猜想在放宽曲率条件下提供了部分肯定结果。

Conclusion: 在适当的对称性条件下，即使将Hopf猜想中的正截面曲率条件放宽为正第二中间里奇曲率，仍然可以保证流形具有正欧拉特征。四周期性定理的扩展为研究此类几何拓扑问题提供了新的工具。

Abstract: Hopf conjectured that even-dimensional closed Riemannian manifolds with
positive sectional curvature have positive Euler characteristic. The conclusion
of the conjecture is known to fail if the positive sectional curvature
assumption is relaxed in any number of ways, including to positive second
intermediate Ricci curvature. Here we prove that if a manifold with positive
second intermediate Ricci curvature has dimension divisible by four and torus
symmetry of rank at least ten, then it has positive Euler characteristic. A
crucial new tool is a non-trivial extension of the first author's Four
Periodicity Theorem to situations where the periodicity of the cohomology does
not extend all the way down to degree zero.

</details>


### [95] [Convexity and the degenerate special Lagrangian equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17018)
*Vasanth Pidaparthy,Yanir A. Rubinstein*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文完全解决了退化特殊拉格朗日方程(DSL)中关于子解凸性的两个开放问题，证明了顶分支子解在时空中的凸性以及第二分支子解的凸性性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 2015年Rubinstein-Solomon提出了退化特殊拉格朗日方程来描述正拉格朗日空间中的测地线，并提出了两个关键问题：顶分支的子解是否在时空中凸，以及第二分支的子解是否具有凸性性质。2019年Darvas-Rubinstein只给出了部分答案，证明了顶分支子解必须是双凸的，但问题仍未完全解决。

Method: 引入了一个关键的新工具——保持时空拉格朗日角的时空坐标变换，并利用这个变换进行部分C²估计。这种坐标变换方法是解决问题的核心技术创新。

Result: 完全解决了两个开放问题：证明了DSL顶分支的子解确实在时空中具有凸性，同时确定了第二分支子解的凸性性质。此外还证明了DSL子方程的前两个分支具有Ross-Witt-Nyström意义下的★-乘积结构。

Conclusion: 通过新的时空坐标变换技术，本文彻底解决了DSL方程中子解凸性的基本问题，为理解正拉格朗日空间中测地线的几何性质提供了完整的理论框架，并揭示了DSL子方程的深层代数结构。

Abstract: In 2015 Rubinstein--Solomon introduced the degenerate special Lagrangian
equation (DSL) that governs geodesics in the space of positive Lagrangians,
showed that subsolutions in the top branch of DSL are convex in space, and
raised the question of whether they should be convex in space-time and whether
subsolutions in the second branch possess any convexity properties. In 2019,
Darvas--Rubinstein gave a partial answer to the first problem by showing
subsolutions in the top branch must be bi-convex. We settle both questions. The
key new ingredient is a space-time coordinate transformation that preserves the
space-time Lagrangian angle and allows for a partial $C^2$ estimate. This also
shows that the top two branches of the DSL subequation have a $\star$-product
structure in the sense of Ross--Witt-Nystr\"om.

</details>

### [99] [Convergence of discrete conformal mappings on surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17037)
*David Glickenstein,Lee Sidbury*

Main category: math.DG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个关于离散保形映射收敛性的一般性定理，扩展了从Thurston圆填充理论开始的离散保形几何研究，证明了重心离散保形映射在适当条件下收敛到连续保形映射。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自1980年代Thurston提出圆填充作为逼近保形映射的方法以来，基于圆填充、顶点缩放等离散保形结构的研究非常活跃。虽然Rodin-Sullivan在1987年证明了圆填充映射确实收敛到圆盘的保形映射，但需要一个更一般的理论框架来处理各种离散保形结构和不同类型的流形（有边界或无边界）之间的映射收敛性问题。

Method: 提出重心离散保形映射（barycentric discrete conformal maps），这是分片线性离散保形映射与黎曼重心坐标的复合。通过对重心离散保形映射的估计来提取收敛子序列，并估计黎曼度量的拉回，从而证明保形性。该方法需要满足单纯形完整性假设以防止退化三角形，以及局部离散保形刚性条件（推广了圆填充的六边形刚性）。

Result: 建立了一个关于曲面间离散保形映射收敛性的一般性定理，该定理适用于多种离散保形结构和有界或无界流形。证明了在适当假设条件下，重心离散保形映射的收敛子序列存在，且其极限映射具有保形性质。

Conclusion: 成功将离散保形映射的收敛理论从特定的圆填充情况推广到更一般的框架，为离散保形几何提供了统一的理论基础。该结果不仅扩展了现有的收敛性结果，还为处理各种离散保形结构和不同类型流形之间的映射提供了有力的理论工具。

Abstract: Discrete conformal mappings based on circle packing, vertex scaling, and
related structures has had significant activity since Thurston proposed circle
packing as a way to approximate conformal maps in the 1980s. The first
convergence result of Rodin-Sullivan (1987) proved that circle packing maps do
indeed converge to conformal maps to the disk. Recent results have shown
convergence of maps of other discrete conformal structures to conformal maps as
well. We give a general theorem of convergence of discrete conformal mappings
between surfaces that allows for a variety of discrete conformal structures and
manifolds with or without boundary. The mappings are a composition of piecewise
linear discrete conformal mappings and Riemannian barycentric coordinates,
called barycentric discrete conformal maps. Estimates of the barycentric
discrete conformal maps allow extraction of convergent subsequences and
estimates for the pullback of the Riemannian metric, proving conformality. The
theorem requires assumptions on fullness of simplices to prevent degenerate
triangles and a local discrete conformal rigidity generalizing hexagonal
rigidity of circle packings.

</details>

### [101] [On rigidity of hypersurfaces with constant shifted curvature functions in warped product manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17344)

Method: 使用积分不等式和Minkowski型公式，研究具有常数线性组合移位高阶平均曲率的超曲面，在子静态翘曲乘积流形中导出刚性定理

Conclusion: 成功将脐点超曲面的刚性理论推广到了更一般的翘曲乘积流形设定中，为微分几何中的刚性问题提供了新的理论工具和方法

Abstract: In this paper, we give some new characterizations of umbilic hypersurfaces in
general warped product manifolds, which can be viewed as generalizations of the
work in \cite{KLP18} and \cite{WX14}. Firstly, we prove the rigidity for
hypersurfaces with constant linear combinations of shifted higher order mean
curvatures. Using integral inequalities and Minkowski-type formulas, we then
derive rigidity theorems in sub-static warped product manifolds, including
cases that the hypersurface satisfies some nonlinear curvature conditions.
Finally, we show that our results can be applied to more general warped product
manifolds, including the cases with non-constant sectional curvature fiber.

</details>

*Tamás Darvas,Nicholas McCleerey*

Abstract: We establish a Ross-Witt Nystr\"om correspondence for weak geodesic lines in

*José Luis Carmona Jiménez*

TL;DR: 研究了Riemannian流形上具有特殊性质的Weyl结构，证明了在Lee形式封闭的完备情况下，Weyl结构必须是平坦的或恰当的，并应用此结果证明了每个齐次Kenmotsu流形都同构于实双曲空间


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Riemannian流形上的Weyl结构，特别是当存在一个余维数为1的∇-平行分布且Lee形式在其上恒等为零时的情况，这种特殊几何结构具有重要的理论意义

Result: 证明了如果(M,g)是完备的且θ是封闭的，那么Weyl结构必须是平坦的或恰当的。应用这一结果证明了每个齐次Kenmotsu流形都与实双曲空间等距同构

Conclusion: 在特定条件下（完备性和Lee形式封闭），Weyl结构的几何性质被严格限制为平坦或恰当，这一结果对齐次Kenmotsu流形的分类具有重要意义，确定了它们都等距于实双曲空间

Abstract: A Weyl structure on a Riemannian manifold $(M,g)$ is a torsion-free linear
connection $\nabla$ such that there is a $1$-form $\theta$ (called the Lee
form) satisfying $\nabla g = 2\, \theta \otimes g$. We examine the case in
which there exists a $\nabla$-parallel distribution of codimension $1$ on which
the Lee form vanishes identically. We prove that if $(M,g)$ is complete with
$\theta$ closed, then the Weyl structure must be flat or exact. We apply this
to show that every homogeneous Kenmotsu manifold is isometric to the real

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于给定的（半黎曼）广义度量和精确Courant代数胚上的散度算子，通过几何构造方法建立规范广义Levi-Civita连接。

scalar-valued curvature invariants, two of which are new.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 4维流形自微分同胚的拓扑伪同伦性质与光滑伪同伦性质并不总是等价的，这种等价性依赖于流形的基本群结构。对于某些特殊的基本群类型等价性成立，但一般情况下不成立

constructed an open domain of discontinuity $\Omega_\rho \subset G/H$, where

discontinuous $\Gamma$-action (via $\rho$) to the space of connections on the

Abstract: We investigate the complexity of the conjugacy problem for fibre products in

$G\twoheadrightarrow Q$. We establish inequalities that relate the conjugator
length function of $P$ to the geometry of cyclic subgroups in $Q$, the Dehn
function of $Q$, the {\em rel-cyclics Dehn function} of $Q$, and the distortion

of finitely generated and finitely presented groups.

### [116] [Collapsi is strongly solved](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16823)
*Michael Young*

Main category: math.HO

TL;DR: 这篇论文分析了一个名为Collapsi的双人完全信息博弈游戏，通过穷举搜索发现先手玩家在37.5%的局面中可以强制获胜，其余情况下后手玩家必胜，游戏最短7步结束，最长14步。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Collapsi是一个新发布的双人完全信息棋类游戏，由于其可能的棋局数量相对较少且博弈树深度较浅，使得对该游戏进行完全的数学分析成为可能，因此研究者希望通过穷举分析来完全解决这个游戏。

Method: 开发了一个求解器，能够在约20毫秒内找到给定棋盘位置的最优移动。通过穷举搜索分析所有可能的对称性破缺后的棋局，计算每种局面下的最优策略和游戏结果。

Result: 研究发现先手玩家可以在37.5%的棋局中强制获胜，后手玩家在其余所有棋局中都能强制获胜。在6.4%的棋局中，失败方可以将游戏延长到最大长度14步；强制获胜最少需要7步。

Conclusion: Collapsi游戏已被完全解决，后手玩家在大多数情况下(62.5%)具有优势，这为游戏设计和博弈论研究提供了有价值的数据。游戏的复杂度适中，既不会过于简单也不会过于复杂。

Abstract: Collapsi is a two-player game of complete information released in June 2025
by Mark S. Ball of Riffle Shuffle & Roll. Played with two pawns on a toroidal
board of 16 randomly mixed playing cards, players take it in turns to move
based on the value of the card they sit on, with the game ending when a player
has no legal moves. The number of possible deals after symmetry breaking is low
enough, and the game tree shallow enough, to make an exhaustive analysis of the
game feasible. A solver was written that can find an optimal move for a given
board position in around 20 milliseconds. A search was applied revealing that
the first player can force a win in 37.5% of deals, with the second player able
to force a win in all others. In 6.4% of deals the losing player can prolong
the game to the maximum length of 14 plies; a win can never be forced in fewer
than 7 plies.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出基于紧凑线性草图的单次扫描算法，利用压缩感知技术构建压缩矩阵测量，然后通过压缩感知恢复算法输出稀疏特征向量近似

Conclusion: 该方法在理论上可证明准确性，在实践中展现了处理超大规模矩阵稀疏特征向量近似的潜力，为大规模数据分析提供了高效解决方案

Abstract: Motivated by applications such as sparse PCA, in this paper we present
provably-accurate one-pass algorithms for the sparse approximation of the top
eigenvectors of extremely massive matrices based on a single compact linear
sketch. The resulting compressive-sensing-based approaches can approximate the
leading eigenvectors of huge approximately low-rank matrices that are too large
to store in memory based on a single pass over its entries while utilizing a
total memory footprint on the order of the much smaller desired sparse
eigenvector approximations. Finally, the compressive sensing recovery algorithm
itself (which takes the gathered compressive matrix measurements as input, and
then outputs sparse approximations of its top eigenvectors) can also be
formulated to run in a time which principally depends on the size of the sought
sparse approximations, making its runtime sublinear in the size of the large
matrix whose eigenvectors one aims to approximate. Preliminary experiments on
huge matrices having $\sim 10^{16}$ entries illustrate the developed theory and
demonstrate the practical potential of the proposed approach.

Abstract: Polarforming is a promising technique that enables dynamic adjustment of

base station (BS) is equipped with polarization-reconfigurable antennas (PRAs)
and can flexibly adjust the antenna polarization to transmit confidential
information to a legitimate user in the presence of an eavesdropper. To
maximize the achievable secrecy rate, we propose an efficient iterative
algorithm to jointly optimize transmit beamforming and polarforming, where
beamforming exploits spatial degrees of freedom (DoFs) to steer the transmit
beam toward the user, while polarforming leverages polarization DoFs to align
the polarization state of the EM wave received by the user with that of its
antenna. Simulation results demonstrate that, compared to conventional
fixed-polarization antenna (FPA) systems, polarforming can fully exploit the
DoFs in antenna polarization optimization to significantly enhance the security
performance of wireless communication systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the problem of distributionally robust source
coding, i.e., source coding under uncertainty in the source distribution,
discussing both the coding and computational aspects of the problem. We propose
two extensions of the so-called Strong Functional Representation Lemma (SFRL),
considering the cases where, for a fixed conditional distribution, the marginal
inducing the joint coupling belongs to either a finite set of distributions or
a Kullback-Leibler divergence sphere (KL-Sphere) centered at a fixed nominal
distribution. Using these extensions, we derive distributionally robust coding
schemes for both the one-shot and asymptotic regimes, generalizing previous
results in the literature. Focusing on the case where the source distribution
belongs to a given KL-Sphere, we derive an implicit characterization of the
points attaining the robust rate-distortion function (R-RDF), which we later
exploit to implement a novel algorithm for computing the R-RDF. Finally, we
characterize the analytical expression of the R-RDF for Bernoulli sources,
providing a theoretical benchmark to evaluate the estimation performance of the
proposed algorithm.

Result: 节点调度方面，该方法在通信预算降低60%的情况下仍能实现更快收敛，始终优于基于中介中心性的方法；在高通信预算（60%以上）时保持相当或更优的性能。链路调度方面，性能优于或等同于MATCHA方法。

Abstract: This paper addresses decentralized stochastic gradient descent (D-SGD) over
resource-constrained networks by introducing node-based and link-based
scheduling strategies to enhance communication efficiency. In each iteration of
the D-SGD algorithm, only a few disjoint subsets of nodes or links are randomly
activated, subject to a given communication cost constraint. We propose a novel
importance metric based on information entropy to determine node and link
scheduling probabilities. We validate the effectiveness of our approach through
extensive simulations, comparing it against state-of-the-art methods, including
betweenness centrality (BC) for node scheduling and \textit{MATCHA} for link
scheduling. The results show that our method consistently outperforms the
BC-based method in the node scheduling case, achieving faster convergence with
up to 60\% lower communication budgets. At higher communication budgets (above
60\%), our method maintains comparable or superior performance. In the link
scheduling case, our method delivers results that are superior to or on par
with those of \textit{MATCHA}.

### [122] [Learning to Write on Dirty Paper](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17427)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的脏纸编码实际实现方案（如Tomlinson-Harashima预编码和基于格的方案）通常依赖于对输入、状态和信道的特定建模假设，而现代学习方法可能为DPC问题提供一条互补的解决路径。

Method: 提出了一种数据驱动的解决方案，其中编码器和解码器都由神经网络参数化。该模型无需事先了解状态（干扰）、信道或输入统计信息，能够恢复产生有效干扰预消除的非线性映射。

Result: 这是第一个可解释的概念验证，证明了基于学习的DPC方案能够恢复已建立解决方案（如THP和基于格的预编码）的特征特性，并在多个场景下优于这些传统方案。

Conclusion: 基于学习的方法可以为脏纸编码问题提供有效的解决方案，神经网络参数化的编解码器能够在无先验知识的情况下实现优于传统方法的性能，为信息论中的经典问题提供了新的实现路径。

Abstract: Dirty paper coding (DPC) is a classical problem in information theory that
considers communication in the presence of channel state known only at the
transmitter. While the theoretical impact of DPC has been substantial,
practical realizations of DPC, such as Tomlinson-Harashima precoding (THP) or
lattice-based schemes, often rely on specific modeling assumptions about the
input, state and channel. In this work, we explore whether modern
learning-based approaches can offer a complementary path forward by revisiting
the DPC problem. We propose a data-driven solution in which both the encoder
and decoder are parameterized by neural networks. Our proposed model operates
without prior knowledge of the state (also referred to as "interference"),
channel or input statistics, and recovers nonlinear mappings that yield
effective interference pre-cancellation. To the best of our knowledge, this is
the first interpretable proof-of-concept demonstrating that learning-based DPC
schemes can recover characteristic features of well-established solutions, such
as THP and lattice-based precoding, and outperform them in several regimes.

</details>


### [123] [Non-Asymptotic Achievable Rate-Distortion Region for Indirect Wyner-Ziv Source Coding](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17432)
*Jiahui Wei,Philippe Mary,Elsa Dupraz*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了间接Wyner-Ziv源编码问题，其中编码器和解码器都无法直接观测到潜在源S，但解码器需要重构S。文章推导了渐近情况下的间接Wyner-Ziv率失真函数，提出了有限块长度下的可达区域，并设计了专门的Blahut-Arimoto算法进行数值评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在目标导向通信背景下，存在一种间接编码场景：编码器需要编码源X，解码器有边信息Y，但同时还需要重构一个编码器和解码器都无法直接观测的潜在源S（如语义信息）。传统的Wyner-Ziv理论无法直接处理这种间接重构问题。

Method: 1) 建立间接Wyner-Ziv源编码的理论框架；2) 推导渐近情况下的间接Wyner-Ziv率失真函数；3) 分析有限块长度情况下的可达区域；4) 设计专门针对间接Wyner-Ziv设置的Blahut-Arimoto算法；5) 将S作为分类标签进行数值实验验证。

Result: 成功推导出间接Wyner-Ziv率失真函数的理论表达式，给出了有限块长度下的可达区域，开发的Blahut-Arimoto算法能够有效计算间接率失真区域。数值实验表明当S被视为分类标签时，该方法能够达到预期的性能。

Conclusion: 本文为间接Wyner-Ziv源编码问题提供了完整的理论分析框架，包括渐近和有限块长度情况下的率失真特性。提出的算法为目标导向通信中的语义信息重构提供了实用的解决方案，为未来的语义通信系统设计奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: In the Wyner-Ziv source coding problem, a source $X$ has to be encoded while
the decoder has access to side information $Y$. This paper investigates the
indirect setup, in which a latent source $S$, unobserved by both the encoder
and the decoder, must also be reconstructed at the decoder. This scenario is
increasingly relevant in the context of goal-oriented communications, where $S$
can represent semantic information obtained from $X$. This paper derives the
indirect Wyner-Ziv rate-distortion function in asymptotic regime and provides
an achievable region in finite block-length. Furthermore, a Blahut-Arimoto
algorithm tailored for the indirect Wyner-Ziv setup, is proposed. This
algorithm is then used to give a numerical evaluation of the achievable
indirect rate-distortion region when $S$ is treated as a classification label.

</details>


### [124] [Bounds and Equivalence of Skew Polycyclic Codes over Finite Fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17571)
*Hassan Ou-azzou,Anna-Lena Horlemann,Nuh Aydin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 研究有限域上的斜多环码，证明了Roos类界限，分析了Hamming和rank等价性，并提供了应用实例

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的多环码理论需要扩展到斜多项式情况，以更好地理解和应用这类编码的性质，特别是在Hamming距离和rank距离下的表现

Method: 通过引入有限域自同态σ，研究与斜多项式f(x)∈𝔽_q[x;σ]相关的斜多环码；建立等价关系来描述不同类别多环码之间的Hamming和rank等价性；证明Roos类型的界限定理

Result: 成功证明了斜多环码在Hamming距离和rank距离下的Roos类界限；建立了两类多环码之间Hamming和rank等价性的理论框架，并描述了其等价类的性质

Conclusion: 为斜多环码提供了完整的理论框架，包括距离界限和等价性分析，所开发的理论具有实际应用价值，为编码理论在该领域的进一步发展奠定了基础

Abstract: We study skew polycyclic codes over a finite field $\mathbb{F}_q$, associated
with a skew polynomial $f(x) \in \mathbb{F}_q[x;\sigma]$, where $\sigma$ is an
automorphism of $\mathbb{F}_q$. We start by proving the Roos-like bound for
both the Hamming and the rank metric for this class of codes. Next, we focus on
the Hamming and rank equivalence between two classes of polycyclic codes by
introducing an equivalence relation and describing its equivalence classes.
Finally, we present examples that illustrate applications of the theory
developed in this paper.

### [125] [On Function-Correcting Codes in the Lee Metric](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17654)
*Gyanendra K. Verma,Abhay Kumar Singh*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文扩展了功能纠错码的研究，从$\mathbb{Z}_{2^l}$上的齐次度量扩展到任意$\mathbb{Z}_m$上的Lee度量，通过引入不规则Lee距离码来确定最优冗余度，并改进了特定函数类别的界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 之前的工作仅研究了$\mathbb{Z}_{2^l}$上使用齐次度量的功能纠错码，需要将这一框架扩展到更一般的$\mathbb{Z}_m$环上的Lee度量，以确定这些码的最优冗余度并改进现有界限。

Method: 引入不规则Lee距离码的概念，通过刻画这类码的最短可能长度来推导最优冗余度的上界和下界，然后将这些一般性界限简化并应用到特定的函数类别上。

Result: 获得了$\mathbb{Z}_m$上Lee度量下功能纠错码最优冗余度的上界和下界，对Lee-局部函数、Lee权重函数和Lee权重分布函数等特定函数类别给出了改进的界限，这些结果改进了Liu和Liu在$\mathbb{Z}_4$上的部分界限并推广了其他界限到一般的$\mathbb{Z}_m$。

Conclusion: 成功将功能纠错码的理论从$\mathbb{Z}_{2^l}$扩展到了一般的$\mathbb{Z}_m$环上的Lee度量，通过不规则Lee距离码确定了最优冗余度的界限，并在多个特定函数类别上取得了理论改进。

Abstract: Function-correcting codes are a coding framework designed to minimize
redundancy while ensuring that specific functions or computations of encoded
data can be reliably recovered, even in the presence of errors. The choice of
metric is crucial in designing such codes, as it determines which computations
must be protected and how errors are measured and corrected. Previous work by
Liu and Liu [6] studied function-correcting codes over $\mathbb{Z}_{2^l},\
l\geq 2$ using the homogeneous metric, which coincides with the Lee metric over
$\mathbb{Z}_4$. In this paper, we extend the study to codes over
$\mathbb{Z}_m,$ for any positive integer $m\geq 2$ under the Lee metric and aim
to determine their optimal redundancy. To achieve this, we introduce irregular
Lee distance codes and derive upper and lower bounds on the optimal redundancy
by characterizing the shortest possible length of such codes. These general
bounds are then simplified and applied to specific classes of functions,
including Lee-local functions, Lee weight functions, and Lee weight
distribution functions, leading to improved some bounds compared to those of
Liu and Liu [6] over $\mathbb{Z}_4$ and generalize the other bounds over
$\mathbb{Z}_m$ in the Lee metric.

</details>


### [126] [Symmetric Private Information Retrieval (SPIR) on Graph-Based Replicated Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17736)
*Shreya Meel,Sennur Ulukus*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究了在复制数据库上的对称私密信息检索(SPIR)问题，其中数据库由简单图建模，建立了一般图的SPIR容量下界，证明了消息特定随机性的最小大小等于消息大小，并推导出路径图和正则图的精确SPIR容量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的私密信息检索研究主要关注完全复制的数据库，但实际应用中数据往往是部分复制的。因此需要研究在图结构建模的复制数据库上的对称私密信息检索问题，其中每个顶点对应一个服务器，消息在两个服务器间复制当且仅当它们之间有边连接。

Method: 提出了一种基于图结构的SPIR模型，其中服务器端的公共随机性也按照图结构在服务器间复制（称为消息特定公共随机性）。通过设计可达到的SPIR方案来建立一般图的SPIR容量下界，并分析SPIR方案可行性的必要条件。

Result: 对于一般图建立了SPIR容量的下界；证明了任何可行SPIR方案的消息特定随机性最小大小必须等于消息大小；通过提供匹配的上界，推导出了路径图和正则图的精确SPIR容量公式。

Conclusion: 本文成功将SPIR问题扩展到了图结构建模的复制数据库场景，建立了理论基础并为特定图类（路径图和正则图）得到了精确的容量结果，为实际分布式存储系统中的隐私保护提供了理论指导。

Abstract: We introduce the problem of symmetric private information retrieval (SPIR) on
replicated databases modeled by a simple graph. In this model, each vertex
corresponds to a server, and a message is replicated on two servers if and only
if there is an edge between them. We consider the setting where the server-side
common randomness necessary to accomplish SPIR is also replicated at the
servers according to the graph, and we call this as message-specific common
randomness. In this setting, we establish a lower bound on the SPIR capacity,
i.e., the maximum download rate, for general graphs, by proposing an achievable
SPIR scheme. Next, we prove that, for any SPIR scheme to be feasible, the
minimum size of message-specific randomness should be equal to the size of a
message. Finally, by providing matching upper bounds, we derive the exact SPIR
capacity for the class of path and regular graphs.

</details>

### [127] [Structures with not too fast unlabelled growth](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16985)
*Bertalan Bodor*

Main category: math.LO

TL;DR: 本文对轨道增长率不超过$\frac{2^n}{p(n)}$的结构类$\mathscr{S}$进行了完整分类，证明了该类结构具有可数性、可在$(\mathbb{Q};<)$中一阶解释等重要性质，并验证了Thomas猜想。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有特定轨道增长率约束的结构类$\mathscr{S}$的分类问题，其中轨道增长率被多项式因子约束，旨在理解此类结构的基本性质和分类特征。

Method: 通过自同构群的角度对结构类$\mathscr{S}$进行完整分类，分析轨道增长率与结构性质之间的关系，运用模型论和代数方法研究结构的可定义性和可解释性。

Result: 证明了$\mathscr{S}$类中的结构在双可定义性意义下只有可数多个，所有这些结构都可以在$(\mathbb{Q};<)$中进行一阶解释，并且与有限有界齐次结构互可定义。此外，还证明了$\mathscr{S}$中的所有结构在互可定义性意义下只有有限多个一阶约简。

Conclusion: 完成了对轨道增长率受多项式约束的结构类$\mathscr{S}$的完整分类，确认了Thomas关于该类结构的猜想，为理解此类数学结构的本质提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: Let $\mathscr{S}$ be the class of all structures whose growth rate on orbits
of subsets of size $n$ is not faster than $\frac{2^n}{p(n)}$ for any polynomial
$p$. In this article we give a complete classification of all structures in
$\mathscr{S}$ in terms of their automorphism groups. As a consequence of our
classification we show that $\mathscr{S}$ has only countably many structures up
to bidefinability, all these structures are first-order interpretable in
$(\mathbb{Q};<)$ and they are interdefinable with a finitely bounded
homogeneous structure. Furthermore, we also show that all structures in
$\mathscr{S}$ have finitely many first-order reduct up to interdefinability,
thereby confirming Thomas' conjecture for the class $\mathscr{S}$.

</details>


### [128] [Algebraic independence of solutions to multiple Lotka-Volterra systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17090)
*Yutong Duan,Christine Eagles,Léo Jimenez*

Main category: math.LO

TL;DR: 本文研究经典Lotka-Volterra系统的代数独立性，证明在特定条件下，不同系统的非退化解在复数域上是代数独立的，并完全分类了非强极小情况下的不变代数曲线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究经典Lotka-Volterra系统解的代数独立性问题，特别是当系统参数满足某些条件时，不同系统的解之间是否存在代数关系。

Method: 1) 扩展Duan和Nagloo的最新工作，证明系统的强极小性；2) 推广Brestovski定理，利用不变体积形式控制代数关系；3) 使用几何稳定性理论的工具分析非强极小情况。

Result: 证明了当$b_i \neq d_i$且$\{b_i, d_i\} \neq \{b_j, d_j\}$时，任意不同非退化解元组$(x_1,y_1), \cdots, (x_m,y_m)$在复数域上代数独立，超越次数为2m。完全分类了$b_i = d_i$情况下的所有不变代数曲线。

Conclusion: 在满足参数条件的情况下，经典Lotka-Volterra系统的不同解具有最大可能的代数独立性，这为理解这类动力系统的代数结构提供了重要理论基础。

Abstract: Consider some non-zero complex numbers $a_i, b_i, c_i, d_i$ with $1 \leq i
\leq n$ and the associated classical Lotka-Volterra systems
  \[
  \begin{cases}
  x' = a_i xy + b_i y \newline
  y' = c_i xy + d_i y \text{ .}
  \end{cases}
  \] We show that as long as $b_i \neq d_i$ for all $i$ and $\{ b_i, d_i\} \neq
\{ b_j, d_j\}$ for $i \neq j$, any tuples $(x_1,y_1) , \cdots , (x_m,y_m)$ of
pairwise distinct, non-degenerate solutions of these systems are algebraically
independent over $\mathbb{C}$, meaning $\mathrm{trdeg}((x_1,y_1) , \cdots ,
(x_m,y_m)/\mathbb{C}) = 2m$. Our proof relies on extending recent work of Duan
and Nagloo by showing strong minimality of these systems, as long as $b_i \neq
d_i$. We also generalize a theorem of Brestovski which allows us to control
algebraic relations using invariant volume forms. Finally, we completely
classify all invariant algebraic curves in the non-strongly minimal, $b_i =
d_i$ case by using machinery from geometric stability theory.

</details>

Conclusion: 本文完善了纠缠线性序的理论，证明了纠缠度形成严格的层次结构，并展示了不同集合论公理对纠缠性质存在性的影响。这些结果深化了对纠缠线性序结构复杂性的理解

Abstract: Entangled linear orders were first introduced by Abraham and Shelah.

\subseteq \mathbb{R}$ such that $A$ is entangled but $B$ is not $2$-entangled.
(3) If $\mathbb{R}\subseteq \mathrm{L}$, then there is an entangled $\Pi_1^1$
set of reals. (4) If $\diamondsuit$ holds, then there is a $2$-entangled
non-separable linear order.

### [132] [Canonical completion and duality for cylindric ortholattices and cylindric Boolean algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17715)
*Joseph McDonald*

Main category: math.LO

TL;DR: 本文研究了圆柱正交格和圆柱布尔代数的代数与拓扑表示理论，建立了圆柱正交格与谱空间某个子范畴之间的对偶等价关系，并获得了在ZF集合论中独立于选择公理的构造性对偶结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的单子正交格和一般正交格的完备化与对偶理论需要扩展到圆柱正交格和圆柱布尔代数的情况，以建立更完整的代数结构表示理论框架。

Method: 通过对圆柱正交格的标准完备化进行研究，在其对偶空间上配备谱拓扑；结合Harding、McDonald和Peinado在单子正交格上的完备化与对偶结果，以及McDonald和Yamamoto在一般正交格上的对偶结果；利用Bezhanishvili和Holliday建立的布尔代数对偶理论来处理圆柱布尔代数。

Result: 证明了圆柱正交格在标准完备化下是封闭的；建立了圆柱正交格范畴与谱空间某个子范畴之间的对偶等价关系；获得了圆柱布尔代数的完备化和对偶结果；所有对偶结果都是构造性的，在ZF集合论中独立于选择公理成立。

Conclusion: 成功建立了圆柱正交格和圆柱布尔代数的完备表示理论，扩展了现有的对偶理论框架，并且所得结果具有构造性特征，在不依赖选择公理的情况下在ZF集合论中成立，为这类代数结构提供了坚实的理论基础。

Abstract: In this note, we investigate the algebraic and topological representation
theory of cylindric ortholattices and cylindric Boolean algebras. The first
contribution demonstrates that cylindric ortholattices are closed under
canonical completions. By equipping a spectral topology to the dual space
associated with the canonical completion, we then establish a dual equivalence
between the category of cylindric ortholattices and a certain subcategory of
the category of spectral spaces. This work builds on the completion and duality
results obtained by Harding, McDonald, and Peinado in the setting of monadic
ortholattices combined with the duality results obtained by McDonald and
Yamamoto in the setting of general ortholattices. By working with the duality
theory for Boolean algebras established by Bezhanishvili and Holliday, we then
obtain completion and duality results for cylindric Boolean algebras. A key
aspect of our duality results is that they are constructive in the sense that
they obtain in Zermelo-Fraenkel set theory independently of the Axiom of
Choice.

### [133] [Orthogonality relations and operators on bounded quasi-implication algebras](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17724)
*Joseph McDonald*

Main category: math.LO

TL;DR: 本文研究了有界拟蕴涵代数的关系和代数性质，构造了单子拟蕴涵代数，并证明了量子单子代数与单子拟蕴涵代数之间存在范畴同构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Hardegree引入的有界拟蕴涵代数的各种关系和代数性质，通过推广MacLaren和Goldblatt在正交格上的构造来探索新的数学结构，并在量子单子代数的框架下研究带有额外算子的拟蕴涵代数。

Method: 通过推广MacLaren和Goldblatt在正交格环境下的构造，从有界拟蕴涵代数构造各种正交关系；引入带有附加算子的有界拟蕴涵代数（称为单子拟蕴涵代数）；利用底层正交模格上的Sasaki蕴涵运算将量子单子代数转换为单子拟蕴涵代数，并反向证明转换的可能性；推广Harding等人在单子正交格上的构造方法。

Result: 证明了每个量子单子代数都可以转换为单子拟蕴涵代数，其底层代数结构由底层正交模格上的Sasaki蕴涵运算确定；反向证明了每个单子拟蕴涵代数都可以转换为量子单子代数；这些构造诱导了量子单子代数范畴与单子拟蕴涵代数范畴之间的同构；成功从单子拟蕴涵代数构造了各种单子正交框架。

Conclusion: 建立了量子单子代数与单子拟蕴涵代数之间的范畴等价关系，证明了这两个数学结构在本质上是等价的，为量子逻辑和代数逻辑的研究提供了新的理论工具和视角。

Abstract: In this note, we study various relational and algebraic aspects of the
bounded quasi-implication algebras introduced by Hardegree. By generalizing the
constructions given by MacLaren and Goldblatt within the setting of
ortholattices, we construct various orthogonality relations from bounded
quasi-implication algebras.
  We then introduce certain bounded quasi-implication algebras with an
additional operator, which we call monadic quasi-implication algebras, and
study them within the setting of quantum monadic algebras. A quantum monadic
algebra is an orthomodular lattice equipped with a closure operator, known as a
quantifier, whose closed elements form an orthomodular sub-lattice. It is shown
that every quantum monadic algebra can be converted into a monadic
quasi-implication algebra with the underlying magma structure being determined
by the operation of Sasaki implication on the underlying orthomodular lattice.
It is then conversely demonstrated that every monadic quasi-implication algebra
can be converted into a quantum monadic algebra. These constructions are shown
to induce an isomorphism between the category of quantum monadic algebras and
the category of monadic quasi-implication algebras.
  Finally, by generalizing the constructions given by Harding as well as
Harding, McDonald, and Peinado in the setting of monadic ortholattices, we
construct various monadic orthoframes from monadic quasi-implication algebras.

</details>

### [134] [Regularity of Resolutions and Limits of Manifolds with a Uniform Contractibility Function](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17557)
*Mohammad Alattar,Lewis Tadman*

Main category: math.MG

TL;DR: 本文提供了Moore 1991年关于有限维Gromov-Hausdorff极限结构猜想的简短自包含证明，并给出了在ANR设置下的应用，包括PL流形和黎曼流形的刻画以及同调流形理论的多个应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 证明Moore在1991年提出的关于某些有限维Gromov-Hausdorff极限结构的猜想，特别是在ANR（绝对邻域收缩核）设置下的情况，并探索其在流形理论中的应用。

Method: 提供了一个简短且自包含的证明方法来解决Moore猜想，通过将问题归约到Bing拓扑学中的已知结果来给出某些经典结果的简短证明，同时还给出了使用更经典论证的另一种证明方法以获得更多结构信息。

Result: 成功证明了Moore猜想，并且能够轻松刻画具有一致可收缩函数的PL流形或黎曼n-流形的有限维极限。对于任何紧连通度量空间（覆盖维数至少为5的可解析ANR同调流形），定义了一个阻碍，该阻碍消失当且仅当同调流形可以在Gromov-Hausdorff意义下被相同维数且具有一致可收缩函数的PL流形逼近。

Conclusion: 该研究为同调流形理论、Alexandrov空间、Wasserstein空间提供了多个应用，并给出了微分同胚稳定性猜想的广义形式，通过归约到Bing拓扑学问题简化了某些已知结果的证明。

Abstract: In this paper, we give a short and self-contained proof to a 1991 conjecture
by Moore concerning the structure of certain finite-dimensional
Gromov--Hausdorff limits, in the ANR setting. As a consequence, one easily
characterizes finite dimensional limits of PL-able or Riemannian $n$-manifolds
with a uniform contractibility function. For example, one can define for any
compact connected metric space that is a resolvable ANR homology manifold of
covering dimension at least 5, an obstruction, which vanishes if and only if
the homology manifold can be approximated in the Gromov--Hausdorff sense by
PL-manifolds of the same dimension and with a uniform contractibility function.
Further, it provides short proofs to certain well known results by reducing
them to problems in Bing topology. We also give another proof using more
classical arguments that yield more structural information. We give several
applications to the theory of homology manifolds, Alexandrov spaces,
Wasserstein spaces and a generalized form of the diffeomorphism stability
conjecture.

</details>

### [135] [The second fluctuation-dissipation theorem for the generalized Langevin equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17350)
*Martin Hanke*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究广义朗之万方程的平稳解存在性，建立了充要条件，并分析了初值问题解的渐近行为和平稳性条件


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究广义朗之万方程平稳解的存在性问题，特别是在记忆核函数作用下的随机微分方程的长时间行为和平稳性特征

Method: 通过对记忆核函数施加适当假设，建立广义朗之万方程二阶平稳解存在的充要条件；将随机方程表述为初值问题，分析波动力项为白噪声和平稳高斯过程组合时的解的性质

Result: 证明了当时间趋于无穷时，解收敛到平稳过程，且极限过程可以是任何具有足够光滑谱密度的中心平稳高斯过程；发现解本身的平稳性需要波动力满足特定的涨落-耗散关系

Conclusion: 广义朗之万方程平稳解的存在性有明确的充要条件，解的平稳性由涨落-耗散关系决定，平稳解由其协方差唯一确定

Abstract: Necessary and sufficient conditions are presented for the existence of
(second order) stationary solutions of the generalized Langevin equation under
appropriate assumptions on the associated memory kernel. When this stochastic
equation is formulated as an initial value problem, then it is shown that the
solution approaches a stationary process as time goes to infinity, whenever the
fluctuating force term is taken to be a combination of a white noise process
and a mean-square continuous centered stationary Gaussian process (which may be
correlated with each other). The limiting process can be any centered
stationary Gaussian process with sufficiently smooth spectral density. On the
other hand, the solution itself is only stationary when the fluctuating force
satisfies a certain fluctuation-dissipation relation, and this stationary
solution is uniquely specified by its covariance.

</details>

*Razvan Gabriel Iagar,David Puertas-Centeno,Elio V. Toranzo*

TL;DR: 本文引入了相对微分-护送变换，基于此定义了双参数相对Fisher测度族和相对累积矩类测度族，并建立了与KL散度和Rényi散度之间的尖锐不等式


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的Fisher测度在缩放变换下不具有不变性，且与经典散度（如KL散度和Rényi散度）之间缺乏尖锐的不等式关系，需要发展更优的测度理论

Method: 引入相对微分-护送变换，通过将变量变化与参考概率密度相关联来扩展传统的微分-护送变换；基于此变换定义双参数相对Fisher测度族和相对累积矩类测度族

Result: 建立了新的相对Fisher测度与KL散度、Rényi散度之间的尖锐不等式；确定了相对累积矩类测度的最优下界及其最小化密度；构造了涉及广义三角函数的不等式族

Conclusion: 相对微分-护送变换提供了一个统一的框架来研究信息测度，新引入的相对Fisher测度具有缩放不变性并与经典散度有尖锐的不等式关系，为信息论和概率论提供了新的理论工具

Abstract: We introduce a new transformation called \emph{relative differential-escort},
which extends the usual differential-escort transformation by relating the
change of variable to a reference probability density. As an application of it,
we define a biparametric family of \emph{relative Fisher measures} presenting
significant advantages with respect to the pre-existing ones in the literature:
invariance under scaling changes and, consequently, sharp inequalities between
the new relative Fisher measure and the well established Kullback-Leibler and
R\'enyi divergences. We also introduce a biparametric family of \emph{relative
cumulative moment-like measures} and we establish sharp lower bounds of these
new measures by the Kullback-Leibler and R\'enyi divergences. The optimal bound
and the minimizing densities are given. We also construct a family of
inequalities for an arbitrary and fixed minimizing density in which the
so-called generalized trigonometric functions plays a central role, providing
thus one more interesting application of the newly introduced inequalities and
measures.

### [137] [Multifold degeneracy points of quantum systems and singularities of matrix varieties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17485)
*György Frank,András Pályi,Gergő Pintér,Dániel Varjas*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究参数依赖量子系统中的多重简并点问题，利用奇点理论方法分析多重简并点在微扰下分解为Weyl点的数量上界，并通过复矩阵空间中几何简并变量的重数计算来确定这一上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参数依赖量子系统常出现能级简并点，当三个或更多能级在同一参数点重合时形成多重简并点。在一般微扰下，这些多重简并点会分解为一系列Weyl点（二重简并点），但分解产生的Weyl点数量缺乏理论上界，需要用奇点理论方法来系统分析这一现象。

Method: 采用奇点理论方法，在复矩阵空间中描述几何简并变量，计算对应多重简并特殊奇点处的重数，以及全纯映射胚相对于该变量的重数，结合局部代数几何工具来确定Weyl点数量的上界。

Result: 成功建立了多重简并点分解产生的Weyl点数量的理论上界，通过几何简并变量在复矩阵空间中的重数计算得到了这一上界的具体表达式，为理解量子系统中多重简并现象提供了数学基础。

Conclusion: 本研究为参数依赖量子系统中多重简并点的分解行为提供了严格的数学框架，建立了Weyl点数量的上界理论，成功架起了物理学和数学两个学科之间的桥梁，为凝聚态物理中的能带结构研究提供了重要的理论工具。

Abstract: Parameter-dependent quantum systems often exhibit energy degeneracy points,
whose comprehensive description naturally lead to the application of methods
from singularity theory. A prime example is an electronic band structure where
two energy levels coincide in a point of momentum space. It may happen, and
this case is the focus of our work, that three or more levels coincide at a
parameter point, called multifold degeneracy. Upon a generic perturbation, such
a multifold degeneracy point is dissolved into a set of Weyl points, that is,
generic two-fold degeneracy points. In this work, we provide an upper bound to
the number of Weyl points born from the multifold degeneracy point. To compute
this upper bound, we describe the geometric degeneracy variety in the space of
complex matrices. We compute its multiplicity at certain singular points
corresponding to a multifold degeneracy, and the multiplicity of holomorphic
map germs with respect to this variety. Our work covers physics and mathematics
aspects in detail, and attempts to bridge the two disciplines and communities.
For self-containedness, we survey examples of multi-fold degeneracies in
quantum systems and condensed-matter physics, as well as the established tools
of local algebraic geometry that we use to identify the upper bound.

</details>

### [139] [Rigidity and positivity of Hawking quasi-local energy on area-constrained critical surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16588)
*Alejandro Peñuela Diaz*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在支配能量条件下，研究霍金能量在面积约束临界面（霍金面）上的性质。对时间对称情况，将霍金面与面积约束威尔莫尔面结合分析；对完全动力学情况，建立新的数学框架进行证明。

Abstract: A key test for any quasi-local energy in general relativity is that it be

enclosed is flat. We show that the Hawking energy, when evaluated on its
natural area-constrained critical surfaces, henceforth called "Hawking
surfaces", satisfies both properties under the dominant energy condition. In
the time-symmetric case, where Hawking surfaces coincide with area-constrained
Willmore surfaces, we extend positivity and rigidity to include electric
charge, a nonzero cosmological constant, and higher dimensions. In the fully
dynamical (non-time-symmetric) case, we establish the first nonnegativity and
rigidity theorems for the Hawking energy in this general setting. These results
confirm the Hawking energy consistency with basic physical principles and
address several longstanding ambiguities and criticisms.

### [141] [Cochain valued TQFTs from nonsemisimple modular tensor categories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17169)
*Agustina Czenky,Cris Negron*

Main category: math.QA

TL;DR: 本文将De Renzi等人构造的向量空间值拓扑量子场论(TQFT)扩展为取值于线性上链对称幺半群范畴的拓扑场论，并进一步局部化为取值于dg向量空间导出∞-范畴的理论。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造一个从带状边界范畴到线性上链范畴的对称幺半群函子。边界范畴的对象是带有模张量范畴Ch(A)标记的曲面，态射是带有嵌入带状图的3维边界。通过保持同伦性质将理论局部化到dg向量空间的导出∞-范畴。

Result: 成功构造了取值于线性上链范畴的TQFT，其中曲面的值被识别为Ch(A)的Hom复形，3-流形不变量是重整化Lyubashenko不变量的交替和。该理论保持同伦并可局部化为∞-范畴值理论。

Conclusion: 本文成功将向量空间值TQFT扩展到上链值理论，并通过局部化得到导出∞-范畴值的理论，为构造量子群表示导出范畴的"导出TQFT"提供了起点和理论基础。

Abstract: We show that a vector space valued TQFT constructed in work of De Renzi et
al. [DGGPR23] extends naturally to a topological field theory which takes
values in the symmetric monoidal category of linear cochains. Specifically, we
consider a bordism category whose objects are surfaces with markings from the
category of cochains Ch(A) over a given modular tensor category (such as the
category of small quantum group representations), and whose morphisms are
3-dimensional bordisms with embedded ribbon graphs traveling between such
marked surfaces. We construct a symmetric monoidal functor from the
aforementioned ribbon bordism category to the category of linear cochains. The
values of this theory on surfaces are identified with Hom complexes for Ch(A),
and the 3-manifold invariants are alternating sums of the renormalized
Lyubashenko invariant from [DGGPR23].
  We show that our cochain valued TQFT furthermore preserves homotopies, and
hence localizes to a theory which takes values in the derived $\infty$-category
of dg vector spaces. The domain for this $\infty$-categorical theory is, up to
some approximation, an $\infty$-category of ribbon bordism with labels in the
homotopy $\infty$-category K(A). We suggest our localized theory as a starting
point for the construction of a "derived TQFT" for the $\infty$-category of
derived quantum group representations.

### [142] [Fourier Transform and the minimal representation of $E_7$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16968)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的特征2域上李超代数有两种不同的定义：带平方映射的Z/2-分次李代数和Verlinde范畴Ver_4^+(k)中的李代数，需要统一这两种概念并建立相应理论

Method: 定义了特征2域k上统一的李超代数概念，证明了PBW（Poincaré-Birkhoff-Witt）定理，研究了限制版本，并通过引入Witt向量环的分歧二次扩张上的混合李超代数概念来研究混合特征变形理论

Result: 成功统一了两种预存的李超代数概念，证明了统一概念下的PBW定理，建立了限制版本的相应理论，并为完美域k建立了混合特征变形理论框架

Conclusion: 通过统一特征2域上的李超代数概念并建立PBW定理，为研究此类代数结构提供了更完整的理论基础；混合李超代数的引入为研究特征2到特征0的变形提供了新的工具和视角

Abstract: We define the notion of a Lie superalgebra over a field $k$ of characteristic
$2$ which unifies the two pre-existing ones - $\mathbb{Z}/2$-graded Lie
algebras with a squaring map and Lie algebras in the Verlinde category ${\rm
Ver}_4^+(k)$, and prove the PBW theorem for this notion. We also do the same
for the restricted version. Finally, discuss mixed characteristic deformation
theory of such Lie superalgebras (for perfect $k$), introducing and studying a
natural lift of our notion of Lie superalgebra to characteristic zero - the
notion of a mixed Lie superalgebra over a ramified quadratic extension $R$ of
the ring of Witt vectors $W(k)$.

</details>

Abstract: In the 90's Soergel constructed a functor that relates Harish-Chandra

### [145] [A Weighted Likelihood Approach Based on Statistical Data Depths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16998)
*Claudio Agostinelli,Ayanendranath Basu,Giulia Bertagnolli,Arun Kumar Kuchibhotla*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于统计深度的加权似然估计方法，通过对异常观测值进行降权处理来获得稳健的参数估计，在无污染情况下保持与最大似然估计相同的渐近效率，同时在污染环境中具有高度稳健性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的最大似然估计对异常值敏感，缺乏稳健性；现有的稳健估计方法（如最小散度估计）在高维情况下需要额外的密度存在性和光滑性假设；需要一种既能保持统计效率又具有稳健性的估计方法，特别是在数据维度随样本量增长的情况下。

Method: 通过修改标准似然方程，引入反映每个数据点相对于模型（而非样本）统计深度的权重；当观测值的模型深度与样本深度差异较大时，对其得分贡献进行降权处理；研究了广泛权重函数类别下估计量的渐近性质，包括一致性和渐近正态性。

Result: 在标准正则性条件下建立了渐近正态性；在无污染情况下达到与最大似然估计相同的渐近效率；在污染环境中保持高度稳健性；即使数据维度随样本量发散也成立，无需额外的密度假设；推导了椭圆对称模型中位置和散布矩阵的有限样本崩溃点。

Conclusion: 提出的加权似然估计量成功结合了统计效率和稳健性，在多元正态模型中表现良好，通过真实数据集和蒙特卡罗模拟验证了方法的有效性，为高维稳健参数估计提供了新的解决方案。

Abstract: We propose a general approach to construct weighted likelihood estimating
equations with the aim of obtaining robust parameter estimates. We modify the
standard likelihood equations by incorporating a weight that reflects the
statistical depth of each data point relative to the model, as opposed to the
sample. An observation is considered regular when the corresponding difference
of these two depths is close to zero. When this difference is large the
observation score contribution is downweighted. We study the asymptotic
properties of the proposed estimator, including consistency and asymptotic
normality, for a broad class of weight functions. In particular, we establish
asymptotic normality under the standard regularity conditions typically assumed
for the maximum likelihood estimator (MLE). Our weighted likelihood estimator
achieves the same asymptotic efficiency as the MLE in the absence of
contamination, while maintaining a high degree of robustness in contaminated
settings. In stark contrast to the traditional minimum divergence/disparity
estimators, our results hold even if the dimension of the data diverges with
the sample size, without requiring additional assumptions on the existence or
smoothness of the underlying densities. We also derive the finite sample
breakdown point of our estimator for both location and scatter matrix in the
elliptically symmetric model. Detailed results and examples are presented for
robust parameter estimation in the multivariate normal model. Robustness is
further illustrated using two real data sets and a Monte Carlo simulation
study.

</details>


### [146] [Approximation Techniques for the Reconstruction of the Probability Measure and the Coupling Parameters in a Curie-Weiss Model for Large Populations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17073)
*Miguel Ballesteros,Ivan Naumkin,Gabor Toth*

Main category: math.ST

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种计算效率高的方法来估计多群体Curie-Weiss模型的耦合参数，避免了传统最大似然估计中分区函数的指数级计算复杂度问题，可应用于政治学、社会学等领域的社会凝聚力分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Curie-Weiss模型最大似然估计需要计算分区函数，其计算复杂度随人口规模呈指数级增长，在实际应用中面临严重的计算瓶颈。需要开发一种能够在常数计算成本下处理任意规模人口的估计方法。

Method: 采用大人口渐近近似方法来计算多群体Curie-Weiss模型概率分布的相关矩，在假设群体间无相互作用的条件下，构建了一个新的耦合参数估计器，该估计器具有常数级的计算复杂度。

Result: 提出的估计器具有一致性（在人口足够大的假设下）、渐近正态性，并满足大偏差原理。估计器的计算成本低且为常数级，不依赖于人口规模大小，可有效应用于政治学、社会学、自动投票等领域。

Conclusion: 研究成功解决了Curie-Weiss模型参数估计的计算复杂度问题，为社会科学中的群体交互现象分析提供了实用的工具。Curie-Weiss模型的耦合参数为社会凝聚力提供了自然的度量标准，该方法在两层投票系统的最优权重估计等实际问题中具有重要应用价值。

Abstract: The Curie-Weiss model, originally used to study phase transitions in
statistical mechanics, has been adapted to model phenomena in social sciences
where many agents interact with each other. Reconstructing the probability
measure of a Curie-Weiss model via the maximum likelihood method runs into the
problem of computing the partition function which scales exponentially with the
population. We study the estimation of the coupling parameters of a multi-group
Curie-Weiss model using large population asymptotic approximations for the
relevant moments of the probability distribution in the case that there are no
interactions between groups. As a result, we obtain an estimator which can be
calculated at a low and constant computational cost for any size of the
population. The estimator is consistent (under the added assumption that the
population is large enough), asymptotically normal, and satisfies large
deviation principles. The estimator is potentially useful in political science,
sociology, automated voting, and in any application where the degree of social
cohesion in a population has to be identified. The Curie-Weiss model's coupling
parameters provide a natural measure of social cohesion. We discuss the problem
of estimating the optimal weights in two-tier voting systems.

</details>

Abstract: We derive the asymptotic distribution of ordinal-pattern frequencies under
weak dependence conditions and investigate the long-run covariance matrix not

coin-tossing processes, but also approximately by a simulation-based approach.
Then, we deduce the asymptotic distribution of the entropy-complexity pair,
which emerged as a popular tool for summarizing the time-series dynamics. Here,
we make the necessary distinction between a uniform and a non-uniform ordinal
pattern distribution and, thus, obtain two different limit theorems. On this
basis, we consider a test for serial dependence and check its finite-sample
performance. Moreover, we use our asymptotic results to approximate the
estimation uncertainty of entropy-complexity pairs.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在两个玩具示例中证明了变分拉普拉斯生成的点估计具有渐近一致性和有效性这些理想性质，推导出了在一般设置下建立这些性质的充分条件，并通过仿真实验验证了理论考虑的有效性。

Abstract: Variational inference is a general framework to obtain approximations to the
posterior distribution in a Bayesian context. In essence, variational inference
entails an optimization over a given family of probability distributions to
choose the member of this family best approximating the posterior. Variational
Laplace, an iterative update scheme motivated by this objective, is widely used
in different contexts in the cognitive neuroscience community. However, until
now, the theoretical properties of this scheme have not been systematically
investigated. Here, we study variational Laplace in the light of frequentist
asymptotic statistics. Asymptotical frequentist theory enables one to judge the
quality of point estimates by their limit behaviour. We apply this framework to
find that point estimates generated by variational Laplace enjoy the desirable
properties of asymptotic consistency and efficiency in two toy examples.
Furthermore, we derive conditions that are sufficient to establish these
properties in a general setting. Besides of point estimates, we also study the
frequentist convergence of distributions in the sense of total variation
distance, which may be useful to relate variational Laplace both to recent
findings regarding variational inference as well as to classical frequentist
considerations on the Bayesian posterior. Finally, to illustrate the validity
of our theoretical considerations, we conduct simulation experiments in our
study examples.

### [149] [Output Feedback Design for Parameter Varying Systems subject to Persistent Disturbances and Control Rate Constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17475)
*Jackson G. Ernesto,Eugenio B. Castelan,Walter Lucia*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对受持续扰动约束的线性参数变化系统的输出反馈控制器设计技术，通过鲁棒正不变集概念和扩展Farkas引理，设计增量参数变化输出反馈控制律来处理控制速率、状态和控制幅值约束问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有控制方法难以同时处理线性参数变化系统中的多重约束问题，包括控制速率约束、状态约束、控制幅值约束，以及系统受到持续扰动和参数变化的影响，需要开发新的输出反馈控制技术来确保系统的鲁棒性和约束满足。

Method: 基于鲁棒正不变集概念，应用扩展Farkas引理推导代数条件来定义控制增益和满足约束的鲁棒正不变多面体；将这些代数条件转化为双线性优化问题，用于确定输出反馈增益和相关的多面体鲁棒正不变区域；在目标函数中包含两个多面体集合的大小，实现外部集合扩大和内部集合最小化的联合优化。

Result: 所获得的控制器确保从多面体出发的任何闭环轨迹在有限时间内收敛到原点周围另一个更小的内部多面体集合，轨迹在该区域内保持最终有界，不受持续扰动和系统参数变化影响；优化方法能够同时扩大外部集合并最小化内部集合；数值实例验证了方法在管理指定约束、扰动和参数变化方面的有效性。

Conclusion: 提出的增量参数变化输出反馈控制方法成功解决了约束线性参数变化系统在持续扰动下的控制问题，通过鲁棒正不变集理论和双线性优化，实现了多重约束的同时满足和系统轨迹的鲁棒收敛，为此类复杂约束控制问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a technique for designing output feedback controllers for
constrained linear parameter-varying systems that are subject to persistent
disturbances. Specifically, we develop an incremental parameter-varying output
feedback control law to address control rate constraints, as well as state and
control amplitude constraints. The proposal is based on the concept of robust
positively invariant sets and applies the extended Farkas' lemma to derive a
set of algebraic conditions that define both the control gains and a robust
positively invariant polyhedron that satisfies the control and state
constraints. These algebraic conditions are formulated into a bilinear
optimization problem aimed at determining the output feedback gains and the
associated polyedral robust positively invariant region. The obtained
controller ensures that any closed-loop trajectory originating from the
polyhedron converges to another smaller inner polyhedral set around the origin
in finite time, where the trajectory remains ultimately bounded regardless of
the persistent disturbances and variations in system parameters. Furthermore,
by including the sizes of the two polyhedral sets inside the objective
function, the proposed optimization can also jointly enlarge the outer set
while minimizing the inner one. Numerical examples are presented to demonstrate
the effectiveness of our proposal in managing the specified constraints,
disturbances, and parameter variations.

### [150] [Distinguishing Phylogenetic Level-2 Networks with Quartets and Inter-Taxon Quartet Distances](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17308)
*Niels Holtgrefe,Elizabeth S. Allman,Hector Baños,Leo van Iersel,Vincent Moulton,John A. Rhodes,Kristina Wicke*

Abstract: The inference of phylogenetic networks, which model complex evolutionary
processes including hybridization and gene flow, remains a central challenge in
evolutionary biology. Until now, statistically consistent inference methods
have been limited to phylogenetic level-1 networks, which allow no
interdependence between reticulate events. In this work, we establish the
theoretical foundations for a statistically consistent inference method for a
much broader class: semi-directed level-2 networks that are outer-labeled
planar and galled. We precisely characterize the features of these networks
that are distinguishable from the topologies of their displayed quartet trees.
Moreover, we prove that an inter-taxon distance derived from these quartets is
circular decomposable, enabling future robust inference of these networks from
quartet data, such as concordance factors obtained from gene tree distributions
under the Network Multispecies Coalescent model. Our results also have novel
identifiability implications across different data types and evolutionary
models, applying to any setting in which displayed quartets can be
distinguished.

### [151] [Exact solution of asymmetric gelation between three walks on the square lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17111)
*Aleksander L Owczarek,Andrew Rechnitzer*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 该研究精确求解了二维三种不同聚合物的非对称接触相互作用模型，分析了具有两种相互作用权重的星形配置下三条定向密切行走的生成函数，发现了四个相的相图并计算了各相的熵指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的对称情况下三条友好行走在西瓜配置中的求解已经成功，但需要研究更复杂的非对称接触相互作用情况，特别是涉及不同类型聚合物的场景，以更好地理解聚合物系统的相行为。

Method: 使用函数方程技术对方格晶格上具有两种相互作用玻尔兹曼权重的三条定向密切行走星形配置进行精确求解，其中顶部一对行走之间有一种接触相互作用，底部一对行走之间有不同的相互作用。

Result: 成功找到了该模型的精确解，阐明了包含四个相的相图，确定了所有相转变的阶数，并计算了每个相中的熵指数。发现密切星形配置比对称情况更适合用函数方程技术进行精确求解。

Conclusion: 通过精确求解非对称接触相互作用的三聚合物模型，揭示了复杂的四相相图结构和相转变性质，证明了密切星形配置在数学处理上的优势，为理解多聚合物系统的统计力学行为提供了重要的理论基础。

Abstract: We find and analyse the exact solution of a model of three different
  polymers with asymmetric contact interactions in two dimensions, modelling a
  scenario where there are different types of polymers involved. In particular,
we find
  the generating function of three directed osculating walks in star
  configurations on the square lattice with two interaction Boltzmann weights,
  so that there is one type of contact interaction between the top pair of
walks and a
  different interaction between the bottom pair of walks. These osculating
  stars are found to be the most amenable to exact solution using functional
  equation techniques in comparison to the symmetric case where three friendly
  walks in watermelon configurations were successfully solved with the same
  techniques. We elucidate the phase diagram, which has four phases, and find
  the order of all the phase transitions between them. We also calculate the
  entropic exponents in each phase.

</details>


### [152] [Exact results for active particle models: from long-range interactions to first-passage properties](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17504)
*Léo Touzo*

Abstract: The goal of this thesis is to obtain new exact results for models of active

combined and extended to derive new results for models of active particles with
long-range interactions. In part two, we study the density of particles in the
stationary state, in the limit where the number of particles is very large,
using an extension of the Dean-Kawasaki equation to run-and-tumble particles
(RTPs). In the case of the 1D Coulomb interaction (attractive or repulsive), we
obtain exact expressions for the stationary density for different types of
confining potentials, which sheds lights on new non-equilibrium
phase-transitions. Some results are also obtained for a repulsive 2D Coulomb
interaction (log-gas), although the single-file constraint makes the study more
difficult in this case. In part three, we focus on the fluctuations at the
tagged particle level. In the limit of weak noise, we compute exactly and
analyze in different regimes a variety of correlation functions of the particle
positions and interparticle distances, both for the Brownian Riesz gas and for
its active counterpart, and show that the activity plays an important role both
at short times and at small distances. The last part of this thesis focuses on
Siegmund duality, which connects the first-passage properties of a stochastic
process with absorbing boundaries to its spatial distribution with hard walls.
We extend this duality to a new class of stochastic processes, which includes
active particles and diffusing diffusivity models.

### [153] [Scaling Properties of Current Fluctuations in Periodic TASEP](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17750)
*Anastasiia Trofimova,Lu Xu*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解驱动相互作用粒子系统中的亚稳态和弛豫动力学，特别是TASEP模型中电流涨落的统计性质和相变行为

Method: 通过参数γ对马尔可夫生成元进行变形，使用坐标Bethe ansatz技术分析控制电流统计的倾斜算子，利用Cassini椭圆的几何结构推导标度累积生成函数和谱隙的隐式表达式

Result: 在热力学极限下发现动力学相变：当γ>0时SCGF呈弹道标度(线性增长)，当γ<0时SCGF收敛到普适常数；谱隙的有限尺寸标度也不同：γ>0时按O(N^-1)关闭，γ<0时指数衰减

Abstract: We investigate current fluctuations in the totally asymmetric simple
exclusion process (TASEP) on a ring of size $N$ with $p$ particles. By
deforming the Markov generator with a parameter $\gamma$, we analyze the tilted
operator governing current statistics using coordinate Bethe ansatz techniques.
We derive implicit expressions for the scaled cumulant generating function
(SCGF), i.e. the largest eigenvalue, and the spectral gap in terms of Bethe
roots, exploiting the geometric structure of Cassini ovals.
  In the thermodynamic limit, at fixed particle density, a dynamical phase
transition emerges between regimes distinguished by the sign of $\gamma$. For
positive deformation $\gamma$, the SCGF exhibits ballistic scaling, growing
linearly with system size $N$. For negative $\gamma$, the SCGF converges to a
universal constant, highlighting distinct fluctuation regimes.
  Correspondingly, the spectral gap, controlling relaxation times, shows
qualitatively different finite-size scaling: it closes as $O(N^{-1})$ for
$\gamma>0$ reflecting slow relaxation, but it decreases exponentially for
$\gamma<0$ indicating rapid convergence. These results provide insight into the
metastability and relaxation dynamics in driven interacting particle systems.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: This paper explores a comprehensive class of time-changed stochastic
processes constructed by subordinating Brownian motion with Levy processes,
where the subordination is further governed by stochastic arrival mechanisms
such as the Cox Ingersoll Ross (CIR) and Chan Karolyi Longstaff Sanders (CKLS)
processes. These models extend classical jump frameworks like the Variance
Gamma (VG) and CGMY processes, allowing for more flexible modeling of market
features such as jump clustering, heavy tails, and volatility persistence. We
first revisit the theory of Levy subordinators and establish strong consistency
results for the VG process under Gamma subordination. Building on this, we

analysis is then extended to the more general CGMY process under stochastic
arrival, for which we derive analogous consistency and limit theorems under
positivity and regularity conditions on the arrival process. A simulation study
accompanies the theoretical work, confirming our results through Monte Carlo
experiments, with visualizations and normality testing (via Shapiro-Wilk
statistics) that show approximate Gaussian behavior even for processes driven
by heavy-tailed jumps. This work provides a rigorous and unified probabilistic
framework for analyzing subordinated models with stochastic time changes, with
applications to financial modeling and inference under uncertainty.

### [157] [How Many Simultaneous Beamformers are Needed for Integrated Sensing and Communications?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.14982)
*Kareem M. Attiah,Wei Yu*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了下行链路集成感知与通信(ISAC)系统中同时实现最佳感知和通信性能所需的最少波束成形器数量，建立了在不同干扰处理能力下的理论界限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在集成感知与通信系统中，基站需要同时进行通信和感知任务，但目前缺乏关于实现两种功能最佳性能所需最少波束成形器数量的理论分析和界限。

Method: 通过理论分析建立波束成形器数量的下界，使用Cramér-Rao界衡量感知性能，用信干噪比衡量通信性能，分别考虑用户能否消除感知波束干扰的两种情况，并将结果扩展到更一般的感知任务。

Result: 当用户能消除感知波束干扰时，最多需要K+√[L(L+1)/2]个波束成形器；当不能消除干扰时，需要√[K²+L(L+1)/2]个。对于复杂路径损耗和到达角估计，在能消除干扰时界限与K和目标数量呈线性关系；不能消除干扰且单目标时，K≥2时仅需K个波束成形器。

Conclusion: 该研究为ISAC系统设计提供了重要的理论指导，表明在某些情况下集成系统所需的波束成形器数量少于各任务独立执行时的总和，证明了ISAC系统设计的效率优势。

Abstract: Consider a downlink integrated sensing and communications (ISAC) system in
which a base station employs linear beamforming to communicate to $K$ users,
while simultaneously uses sensing beams to perform a sensing task of estimating
$L$ real parameters. How many beamformers are needed to achieve the best
performance for both sensing and communications? This paper establishes bounds
on the minimum number of downlink beamformers, in which sensing performance is
measured in terms of the Cram\'{e}r-Rao bound for parameter estimation and
communications performance is measured in terms of the
signal-to-interference-and-noise ratios. We show that an ISAC system requires
at most $K + \sqrt{\frac{L(L+1)}{2}}$ beamformers if the remote users have the
ability to cancel the interference caused by the sensing beams. If cancelling
interference due to the sensing beams is not possible, the bound becomes
$\sqrt{K^2 + \frac{L(L+1)}{2}}$. Interestingly, in the latter case, the bound
on the number of beamformers is less than the sum of the bounds for each task
individually. These results can be extended to sensing tasks for which the
performance is measured as a function of $d$ quadratic terms in the
beamformers. In this case, the bound becomes $K + \sqrt{d}$ and $\sqrt{K^2 +
d}$, respectively. Specifically, for estimating complex path losses and
angles-of-arrival of $N_\text{tr}$ targets while communicating to $K$ users,
the bound on the minimum number of beamformers scales linearly in $K$ and in
$N_\text{tr}$, assuming interference from sensing can be cancelled. When
interference cancellation is not possible, the following exact characterization
for the case of $N_\text{tr} = 1$ can be obtained: when $K=0$ or $1$, two
beamformers should be used; when $K \ge 2$, exactly $K$ beamformers should be
used, i.e., communication beamformers alone are already sufficient.

</details>

### [160] [Fundamental limits of distributed covariance matrix estimation via a conditional strong data processing inequality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16953)
*Mohammad Reza Rahmani,Mohammad Hossein Yassaee,Mohammad Reza Aref*

Main category: stat.ML

TL;DR: 本文研究了在特征分割设置下分布式协方差矩阵估计的理论极限，提出了条件强数据处理不等式(C-SDPI)系数，并建立了几乎紧致的minimax下界，同时设计了接近最优的估计协议。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维协方差矩阵估计是许多领域的关键任务，在通信受限的分布式环境下，需要理解估计精度与通信成本之间的理论权衡关系，现有文献多假设无限样本或高斯分布，缺乏更一般的理论框架。

Method: 引入条件强数据处理不等式(C-SDPI)系数作为主要技术工具，该系数具有张量化等关键性质，能量化状态依赖信道中的平均收缩；结合Geng-Nair的倍增技巧和算子Jensen不等式计算高斯混合信道的系数；建立minimax下界并设计相应的估计协议。

Result: 获得了算子范数和Frobenius范数下协方差矩阵估计的几乎紧致minimax下界；提出的估计协议在样本和通信要求上与下界仅相差对数因子；证明了交互式协议相比非交互式方案能显著降低通信需求；框架不依赖无限样本或高斯分布假设。

Conclusion: 本文建立了分布式协方差估计的理论基础，揭示了样本大小、通信成本和数据维度之间的根本权衡关系，提供了广泛适用的理论框架，并证明了交互通信的优势。

fields. This paper explores the theoretical limits of distributed covariance
estimation in a feature-split setting, where communication between agents is
constrained. Specifically, we study a scenario in which multiple agents each
observe different components of i.i.d. samples drawn from a sub-Gaussian random
vector. A central server seeks to estimate the complete covariance matrix using
a limited number of bits communicated by each agent. We obtain a nearly tight
minimax lower bound for covariance matrix estimation under operator norm and
Frobenius norm. Our main technical tool is a novel generalization of the strong
data processing inequality (SDPI), termed the Conditional Strong Data
Processing Inequality (C-SDPI) coefficient, introduced in this work. The C-SDPI
coefficient shares key properties such as tensorization with the conventional
SDPI. Crucially, it quantifies the average contraction in a state-dependent
channel and can be significantly lower than the worst-case SDPI coefficient
over the state input.
  Utilizing the doubling trick of Geng-Nair and an operator Jensen inequality,
we compute this coefficient for Gaussian mixture channels. We then employ it to
establish minimax lower bounds on estimation error, capturing the trade-offs
among sample size, communication cost, and data dimensionality. Building on
this, we present a nearly optimal estimation protocol whose sample and
communication requirements match the lower bounds up to logarithmic factors.
Unlike much of the existing literature, our framework does not assume infinite
samples or Gaussian distributions, making it broadly applicable. Finally, we
extend our analysis to interactive protocols, showing interaction can
significantly reduce communication requirements compared to non-interactive
schemes.

</details>


<div id='hep-th'></div>

Motivation: 理解量子格点规范理论中高阶形式对称性和't Hooft反常的代数结构，特别是这些对称性在空间区域限制下的行为

Method: 采用同伦论和算子代数方法，通过考虑对称变换在空间区域上的限制来研究高阶形式对称性，将这些限制数据打包成高阶群结构，并使用交叉群立方体的代数模型

information is encoded in a crossed square of groups, which is an algebraic
model of a 3-group. In general, we propose that higher groups appear in lattice
models and QFT as crossed n-cubes of groups via a nonabelian version of the

### [163] [The sphere free energy of the vector models to order $1/N$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16896)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决Tarnopolsky在arXiv:1609.09113中提出的关于球面自由能计算的理论难题，特别是如何正确处理这些共形场论中的紫外发散和正规化问题。

Method: 使用大N展开技术计算球面自由能，通过一致性地移动辅助场的紫外标度维度来进行解析正规化，修改其动力学项，并结合反项来处理发散问题。

Result: 成功计算了O(N) φ⁴和Gross-Neveu CFTs的球面自由能至1/N阶，结果与ε展开匹配，解决了之前的理论矛盾。发现这些自由能可以用反常维度紧凑地表示，适用于短程和长程版本的CFTs。

Conclusion: 通过修改辅助场的动力学项实现了一致的解析正规化，解决了Tarnopolsky难题。发现长程CFT在其修正自由能作为矢量标度维度函数达到最大值时，恰好转变为短程CFT，揭示了两种理论之间的深层联系。

Abstract: We calculate the large-$N$ expansion of the sphere free energy $F=-\log
Z_{S^d}$ of the O(N) $\phi^4$ and the Gross-Neveu $(\bar{\psi} \psi)^2$ CFTs to
order $1/N$. Analytical regularization of these theories requires consistently
shifting the UV scaling dimension of the auxiliary field: this can only be done
by modifying its kinetic term. This modification combines with the counterterms
to give the result that matches the $\epsilon$-expansion, resolving a puzzle
raised by Tarnopolsky in arXiv:1609.09113. These $F$s can be written compactly
in terms of the anomalous dimensions, for both the short-range and the
long-range versions of these CFTs. We also provide various technical results
including a computation of the counterterms on the sphere and a neat derivation
of the sphere free energy of a free conformal field. Finally, we observe that
the long-range CFT becomes the short-range CFT at exactly the point where its
$\tilde{F} =-\sin \tfrac{\pi d}{2} F$ is maximized as a function of the
vector's scaling dimension.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了计算传递算子谱性质的算法，避免谱污染问题，并将方法扩展到Hardy-Hilbert空间。通过函数解析的方法处理"真实"Koopman谱的定义问题

Result: 通过多个案例研究验证了方法的准确性和灵活性，包括已知谱的Blaschke映射族和蛋白质折叠的分子动力学模型。证明了即使对应的特征函数不在选择的空间内，谱特征仍可能出现

Abstract: Koopman operator theory enables linear analysis of nonlinear dynamical
systems by lifting their evolution to infinite-dimensional function spaces.
However, finite-dimensional approximations of Koopman and transfer
(Frobenius--Perron) operators are prone to spectral pollution, introducing
spurious eigenvalues that can compromise spectral computations. While recent
advances have yielded provably convergent methods for Koopman operators,
analogous tools for general transfer operators remain limited. In this paper,
we present algorithms for computing spectral properties of transfer operators
without spectral pollution, including extensions to the Hardy-Hilbert space.
Case studies--ranging from families of Blaschke maps with known spectrum to a
molecular dynamics model of protein folding--demonstrate the accuracy and
flexibility of our approach. Notably, we demonstrate that spectral features can
arise even when the corresponding eigenfunctions lie outside the chosen space,
highlighting the functional-analytic subtleties in defining the "true" Koopman
spectrum. Our methods offer robust tools for spectral estimation across a broad
range of applications.

### [165] [Exactness, Cohomology, and Uniqueness in First-Order Differential Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.16457)
*Hemanta Mandal*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文通过德拉姆上同调研究一阶微分方程的可解性与其定义域拓扑结构之间的关系，证明了第一德拉姆上同调群的平凡性是全局可积性和解唯一性的根本要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过德拉姆上同调理论分析与一阶ODE相关的闭1-形式是否存在全局势函数，将问题归结为微分形式的恰当性。在实射影平面ℝP²等非单连通流形上构造显式例子，并与ℝ²\{0}等域进行比较，研究积分因子与上同调类平凡化的对应关系。

Result: 证明了第一德拉姆上同调群H¹_dR的平凡性是全局可积性和解唯一性的根本要求。展示了某些非单连通流形（如实射影平面ℝP²）由于H¹_dR的消失仍然支持全局解。揭示了拓扑障碍如何在解析上表现为非唯一性或多值行为。

Conclusion: 建立了几何、拓扑和解析视角的统一框架，用于理解一阶常微分方程超越局部存在定理的全局行为。第一德拉姆上同调群的平凡性，而非单连通性，是决定全局解存在性的关键拓扑条件。

Abstract: This paper investigates the relationship between the solvability of
first-order differential equations and the topology of the underlying domain
through the lens of de\,Rham cohomology. We analyze the conditions under which
a closed 1-form associated with a first-order ODE admits a global potential,
thereby reducing the problem to the exactness of differential forms. While it
is well known that exactness is guaranteed on simply connected domains, we show
that triviality of the first de\,Rham cohomology group is the more fundamental
requirement for global integrability and uniqueness of solutions. In
particular, we demonstrate that certain non-simply connected manifolds, such as
the real projective plane $\mathbb{RP}^2$, still support global solutions due
to the vanishing of $H^1_{\text{dR}}$. By explicitly constructing examples on
$\mathbb{RP}^2$ and comparing them with domains like $\mathbb{R}^2 \setminus
\{0\}$, we illustrate how topological obstructions manifest analytically as
non-uniqueness or multi-valued behavior. We further discuss the correspondence
between integrating factors and the trivialization of cohomology classes,
drawing connections to classical symmetry methods and potential theory. This
synthesis of geometric, topological, and analytic perspectives provides a
unifying framework for understanding the global behavior of first-order ODEs
beyond local existence theorems.

### [168] [Relational Quantum Dynamics (RQD): An Informational Ontology](https://arxiv.org/abs/2412.05979)

Main category: quant-ph

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出关系量子动力学(RQD)解释，基于五个相互关联的原理：(1)量子态是情境性和观察者相对的；(2)时间从量子相互作用中涌现；(3)空间由量子纠缠模式构建；(4)观察者作为高度集成信息的系统涌现；(5)经典现实通过量子退相干出现。该方法否认单一的观察者独立现实，用关系的、情境依赖的真理替代绝对事实。

Conclusion: RQD可能提供了一个统一图景，其中量子力学、时空和观察者不再是分离的领域，而是一个相互连接的信息网络的不同方面。这种解释将关系和信息置于物理学基础地位，为理解现实的本质提供了新的框架。

Abstract: Quantum mechanics has transformed our understanding of reality, yet deep
philosophical puzzles remain unresolved. Is there a consistent way to describe
quantum measurement, the emergence of space and time, and the role of observers
within one coherent ontology? This paper introduces Relational Quantum Dynamics
(RQD), an interpretation that places relationships and information, not
isolated objects, at the foundation of physics. Unlike traditional views, such
as the Copenhagen interpretation, Everett's many-worlds theory, or
hidden-variable approaches, RQD denies a single observer-independent reality,
instead proposing that facts only become definite within specific observational
contexts. It explicitly addresses foundational no-go results, including Bell's
theorem, the Kochen-Specker theorem, and the Frauchiger-Renner paradox, by
replacing absolute facts with relational, context-dependent truths. RQD rests
on five interlocking principles: (1) quantum states are contextual and
observer-relative, (2) time emerges from quantum interactions rather than
existing as an external parameter, (3) space is constructed from patterns of
quantum entanglement, (4) observers emerge as systems with highly integrated
information, and (5) classical reality appears through quantum decoherence
without special wavefunction collapse. Philosophically, RQD aligns with ontic
structural realism, proposing that the fundamental ontology of the universe
consists entirely of informational relations. It avoids collapsing into
relativism or solipsism by ensuring intersubjective agreement through physical
interactions. Ultimately, RQD may offer a unified picture in which quantum
mechanics, spacetime, and observers are no longer separate domains but aspects
of one interconnected informational web.

### [169] [Quantitative Quantum Soundness for Bipartite Compiled Bell Games via the Sequential NPA Hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17006)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 对具有有限维最优量子策略的双方编译贝尔博弈建立量化量子可靠性界限；2) 引入并形式化序列Navascués-Pironio-Acín (NPA)层次结构；3) 分析无限维最优策略博弈的NPA近似误差必要性。

Conclusion: 成功建立了编译贝尔博弈的首个量化量子可靠性界限，提供了实用的序列NPA层次结构数值工具，并揭示了无限维情况下与复杂性理论和量子同态加密的深层联系。

Abstract: Compiling Bell games under cryptographic assumptions replaces the need for
physical separation, allowing nonlocality to be probed with a single untrusted
device. While Kalai et al. (STOC'23) showed that this compilation preserves
quantum advantages, its quantitative quantum soundness has remained an open
problem. We address this gap with two primary contributions. First, we
establish the first quantitative quantum soundness bounds for every bipartite
compiled Bell game whose optimal quantum strategy is finite-dimensional: any
polynomial-time prover's score in the compiled game is negligibly close to the
game's ideal quantum value. More generally, for all bipartite games we show
that the compiled score cannot significantly exceed the bounds given by a newly
formalized sequential Navascu\'es-Pironio-Ac\'in (NPA) hierarchy. Second, we
provide a full characterization of this sequential NPA hierarchy, establishing
it as a robust numerical tool that is of independent interest. Finally, for
games without finite-dimensional optimal strategies, we explore the necessity
of NPA approximation error for quantitatively bounding their compiled scores,
linking these considerations to the complexity conjecture
$\mathrm{MIP}^{\mathrm{co}}=\mathrm{coRE}$ and open challenges such as quantum
homomorphic encryption correctness for "weakly commuting" quantum registers.

### [170] [A Unified Toolbox for Multipartite Entanglement Certification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2507.17435)

Method: 基于条件梯度（CG）方法构建统一框架，结合快速启发式检测和严格的见证函数构造，并具有数值误差控制能力。该方法适用于任意纠缠结构，并扩展到一般量子噪声信道下的纠缠鲁棒性分析。

Result: 成功实现了多达十个量子比特系统的纠缠认证；在束缚纠缠态的白噪声鲁棒性基准测试中缩小了纠缠与可分离性界限的差距；在超出先前算法方法范围的情况下提供了准确的阈值。

Conclusion: 条件梯度方法为实际实验环境中的纠缠分析提供了强大且可扩展的工具，能够有效处理复杂的多体量子系统和噪声环境下的纠缠表征问题。

Abstract: We present a unified framework for multipartite entanglement characterization
based on the conditional gradient (CG) method, incorporating both fast
heuristic detection and rigorous witness construction with numerical error
control. Our method enables entanglement certification in quantum systems of up
to ten qubits and applies to arbitrary entanglement structures. We demonstrate
its power by closing the gap between entanglement and separability bounds in
white noise robustness benchmarks for a class of bound entangled states.
Furthermore, the framework extends to entanglement robustness under general
quantum noise channels, providing accurate thresholds in cases beyond the reach
of previous algorithmic methods. These results position CG methods as a
powerful tool for practical and scalable entanglement analysis in realistic
experimental settings.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: As quantum hardware rapidly advances toward the early fault-tolerant era, a

with a provable runtime guarantee. Our algorithm uses only a single ancilla
qubit, and is locality preserving, i.e., when the coefficient matrix of the ODE

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 拓扑相、边缘态和平带是拓扑量子计算和抗噪声信息处理的关键资源。现有方法通常需要复杂的分步或分币协议，本文旨在开发一种更简单高效的方案来模拟这些拓扑现象。

Method: 提出基于循环图上步长相关量子行走的循环量子行走(CQWs)方案，使用离散傅里叶变换和有效哈密顿量。通过奇偶位点循环图的不同谱特征，在4n位点图上生成旋转对称平带，并在不同拓扑相界面处构造受保护的边缘态。

Result: 成功生成了有隙和无隙拓扑相，包括狄拉克锥样能量色散、拓扑非平凡平带和受保护边缘态。证明了旋转空间中的能隙闭合意味着动量空间中狄拉克锥的形成。数值验证表明边缘态对中等静态和动态门无序具有鲁棒性，并在保相扰动下保持稳定。

Conclusion: 该方案为量子系统中工程拓扑相、相变、边缘态和平带提供了资源高效且多功能的平台，为容错量子技术开辟了新的途径，具有重要的理论和应用价值。

Abstract: Topological phases, edge states, and flat bands in synthetic quantum systems
are a key resource for topological quantum computing and noise-resilient
information processing. We introduce a scheme based on step-dependent quantum
walks on cyclic graphs, termed cyclic quantum walks (CQWs), to simulate exotic
topological phenomena using discrete Fourier transforms and an effective
Hamiltonian. Our approach enables the generation of both gapped and gapless
topological phases, including Dirac cone-like energy dispersions, topologically
nontrivial flat bands, and protected edge states, all without resorting to
split-step or split-coin protocols. Odd and even-site cyclic graphs exhibit
markedly different spectral characteristics, with rotationally symmetric flat
bands emerging exclusively $4n$-site graphs ($n\in \mathbf{N}$). We
analytically establish the conditions for the emergence of topological, gapped
flat bands and show that gap closings in rotation space imply the formation of
Dirac cones in momentum space. Further, we engineer protected edge states at
the interface between distinct topological phases in both odd and even cycle
graphs. We numerically demonstrate that the edge states are robust against
moderate static and dynamic gate disorder and remain stable against
phase-preserving perturbations. This scheme serves as a resource-efficient and
versatile platform for engineering topological phases, transitions, edge
states, and flat bands in quantum systems, opening new avenues for
fault-tolerant quantum technologies.
